et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the fire cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lard and mix it with old oil, and place it on the hollow area between the base of the thumb and the other that is called a flexor.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry donkey bile, immerse it in fire until it turns into charcoal, and place it on the wool, and leave it until it becomes soot.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And do it again this way, and never stop doing it until you think by sense that it will reach the hip, and the pain be gone.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this method of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	The pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or impact, or due to too much evacuation, or because of cold matter spread out, none of these occurrences warrants cauterization, rather it is for someone who has come from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After that, when the patient is void of foul pills or other similar things, one should perform this on their back, at the spot where the pain resides, three lines indicating across, and in each line V cauterizations or more according to the virtue and quantity the illness can withstand;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And the cauterizations should be done according to the method called "points" for the cauterization.
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see fit, perform three or four cauterizations at the middle of the wrist cauterization in this manner:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness often befalls young children, and the symptoms of its onset are that they have pale skin when they stand up, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the last spinal vertebra of the back and with us the appearance that comes over other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe it being treated, if you apply the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery is applied to each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see fit, apply the fire cautery to each side of the spine with two or three lines of heat, and ensure the points are close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the treatment until it is clean according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply heat in a state of fever where there might be nerve inflammation.
de la dolor des jointes	of joint pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain is due to moistures that spread throughout each body part, and when pain comes in the feet, which they call 'gout' properly, and when it's caused by cold and cannot be cured by medicine alone, but must be treated with cauteries in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the mouth of the cautery at the joint of the foot, and apply the olive oil in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there's need that you touch the back of the foot, if it is heated to the full heat of what we call 'a point'.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains extend up to the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, then apply cautery on each knee for three or four of them, using all olive oil;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need to do more, then do so, but don't let your hand stray beyond the point until the wound's healing is complete.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains go down to the knees and back, then administer the cautery as we have said in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then do points within the inner forearm lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there remains any pain in the elbows, then do points on each joint and on the back of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains come up to the shoulders or down to the elbows, then cauterize each part, and give good guidance to the patient and prescribe medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	And if you take good care of him and cleanse the humor, he will be helped by God to recovery.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the spleen
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When the stomach is upset and the bile descends into the kidneys (indicating dyspepsia), if it's a new case, you must ensure that when you see them to cure, they should not fast on that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And when he eats things that ease his stomach, so that his insides descend from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After you have him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to mark his armpit until the hair is repaired, then pinch it with your fingers, and watch for signs beneath the wound on the bone, and at every sign make it resemble half of a circle above the chest;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then prepare the cautery as described:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and emits pus.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then pinch the hairs at their base;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And have the attendants mark his hand so that it does not turn back;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And work well on the thighs with the assistant, and place wool and surgeon on the thighs, and another near his anus so that he marks his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery at the sign on every part of your hand, and keep it straight and hold it until you touch the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, try again several times until you arrive at the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and remember that the oil should not spill when you apply the heat of the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so as not to burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that through this the patient does not die, or suffer from any other ailments.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach bone with the cautery, your operations are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	It is necessary that the cauterization for children be subtle according to their size, and likewise for adults as large as their size allows.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, cure the wound with butter until the scab is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After performing other treatments until he is well, let the patient rest for forty days on his back so that the wound heals properly.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that these purges be taken for a long time, so that the urine does not overflow when he wishes to go into chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wants to stand up, have him wear a well-made bandage, and let him do this for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And have him get good rest, so that he does not overwork himself and avoids excessive drinking or eating, as well as shouting too loudly;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he follows this instruction, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after about the treatment of tailoring in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When abscesses occur in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, apply the fire cautery gently according to its quantity, and make it heat for one third of the cup.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And none of the old ones said that one should use the cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But the first sign is the beginning of an infection and draw a line across the width above the incision, and another below, and hold your hand in contact with the entire length of the cauterized area.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and more moist.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in no limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, or due to falling or being hit, and this pain lasts for a long time, and medical treatment does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "points", and apply the cauterizations according to the length of the limb, its smallness, its weakness, its utility, and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is correctly done with the first cautery, it's well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it's named, start with another cautery on that one, because such injuries are accustomed to cause movement in the body part closest to them, so you should apply the cauterizations as long as the patient is still.
de meselerie	In mixture
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The remedies are administered once per heat treatment by great help, and similarly, the disease comes from the putrefaction of blood and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can't you see the cauterization? Take care that the disease is at the beginning, and if it is treated according to what we have said in this section, without spreading or remaining, and you fear that the infection will spread throughout the patient's body, then apply five cauterizations on its head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I lead the head to nine, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hair.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and II above II horns, and I behind on the hinder part;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I let my hand remain as the cautery comes until it reaches the bone, and as long as the scabs come out so that the vapors of the large fluids can escape;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and apply cautery to the mouse according to how it is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the infection is spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And when it is clearly spreading, it is necessary that you apply these cauterizations with the cautery as we have described: first to the head and then on the neck spine, two on each shoulder blade, six on the back spine, one large on the rump and another behind, and two on each of the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	And on the heels, and on the tendons beneath the foot, and in each joint of hands and feet, and in the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	And guard against the nerves that lie under the heel part, so as not to burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And never apply the cautery to the bone of the hand, and once on the bone of the stomach, and another time on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that with every application of the cautery, I am aiding it more, and it gains from that use;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the patients do not feel pain during the cautery as those who are healthy would, because their body is already thoroughly corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the size of the cautery be large and small according to the limbs and joints, as you will find in methods for metalworking.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, wash the wound with flour mixed with honey and other remedies until it heals properly.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When any part swells and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters but does not improve, then I make cauterizations to the limb according to its size and the extent of the swelling;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cauterizing fire slightly penetrate the skin of the scrotum;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply the salve until it heals properly.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And one should cauterize with the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that makes the limb move. In this way, the swelling is released;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And yet, do not interfere with it unless you are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	From galls
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is advanced, and medicine does not help, then cauterize with a slightly intense fire according to the amount of scrotum skin, until the swelling is released, and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then apply a paste of flour and lentils mixed with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood from hog and blood from dove, using equal parts of each.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And mix all together, and bind it with a bandage, and let it air on the wound until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment for a pustule by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the gangrene begins and you see it stop, if you notice it, then apply the cautery to the point that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the gangrene.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And indeed, they advised that one should also cauterize in the middle of the ulcer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And indeed, I do not think this is good either, for fear that it might become ulcerated and decayed, and I have already decided never to try this method;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And more correct is to cauterize internally, with the cautery that is called "circular", as we have said in the context of various cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling which cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some have a disease that is called "adubelati", and it delays death or due to the excess it makes or because of age during illness (that means too old), when there is little blood, or due to the weak health;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hastening towards death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	therefore, apply the cautery around that area with small fires and pressing on them;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards let it be this way.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it being pierced through the entire cauterization, then heat the cauterizing instrument as described here:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease that is called 'adubelati' until the cauterizations penetrate the body, and make the cauterizations such that the patient feels an escape in this manner that the process of decomposition be relieved.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure using fire through a iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called 'corrodens', and it's not another thing but a member infirmity, for it causes members to behave as if they were dry branches that the fire has burnt.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in them that can endure a combined fire cautery, then apply small and large fire cauteries like a chain link, according to what is needed for the area or where the illness is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After applying the cautery from all sides until you remove all the corruption, and leave nothing of it, that every part which is corrupted be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And let it rest for three days, and apply soothing ointment with oil on the burned areas until the scabs from the fire have healed, and ensure all the corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the cure of ointments that produce pus.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after three days you see that there is no sign of health emerging, this is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if not, reapply the cautery to what remains of the ear that is decayed.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this cure has been treated with medical remedies instead of a fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	However, the fire cautery is much more effective, and I have already discussed the use of medical remedies in that section.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take what you need when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of ulcers that come on bones
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Sometimes, when there is an opening in the foot, it leads to a disease that we call "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large hard lump that causes pain in the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterizations for this disease can be done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This is to know about fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	A fire cautery if you're using it should be shaped like a needle, just as one would draw with feathers. Make sure it's well made of iron to the size that it can accommodate nails in every direction, and ensure it has small edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After warming it all up on the hot iron, and turn your hand completely around the iron rod until it reaches to the very end of the rod.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it like this for three days until signs of putrefaction begin;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make him a poultice of powdered wild mustard with vinegar, and let the poultice on overnight, and nail it firmly so that it is uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with greasing until it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they turn from the back of the heart, and it happens many times in both hands and knees, then you should bring them a hot water cautery;
et est en teil maniere:	and is done like this:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take an arnica stick or a iron rod, or a feather of a goose, and place it on the stake and the althelul, meaning for warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the torch on it until it blackens all around, then I put a little hot ash, and keep your hand firmly, press your hand as you turn that the edge of the torch turns towards the base of the nail, and then find the hot water's deep passage to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	And let the patient endure a little bit of the hot water's burn for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then leave it like that, and it will uproot completely from all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do this for one after the other, until you have cleared all those that are in your body, then treat the sores that generate pus.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment involves shaking it off.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When there's a trembling due to cold or nerves, or a fever of the fourth kind or other maladies, it is necessary that you perform four or four cauterizations on the spinal column of the back, one cautery between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	And for the fire cautery, place it on the stomach with the olive cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If it causes trembling, and hasten the cure of the cold illness.
des pustules puans	The pus-filled lesions
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	In every instance where a dead body is exposed or oozing sores, or pus-filled bumps appear, these come from large putrid materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	It is necessary at the beginning when they appear that one applies a cautery to each head of the pimple:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A fine cautery of elm wood, whose points are taken by fire, or from the root of the asarum long, or with the lentis-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And each time they cauterize, at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow pus forward but remove the excess that comes from them, and become healthy;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But it must be done after the blood has been evacuated.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times great bloodflows from the artery which is cut at the wound, leading to backflow or at the incision of an abscess, or during the application of a fire cautery on the limb, and similar situations;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very difficult to smell such things.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet, when such an event happens to none of them, if you quickly place your index finger on the wound in the vein, and press it so that the pulse stops under your finger, and no more drop comes out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then apply several small and large olive fire cauterizers until they turn completely red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then take one, whether large or small depending on the wound and where the artery runs, and place the cauterizer on that vein where you have your finger, and hold the cauterizer there until the pulse stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you remove your finger from the vein, and once the cauteries are extinguished, take quickly another one of the cauterizing tools that are at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop performing this one after another until the skin is completely healed;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and see to it that you do not burn the nerve beneath, and that no other mischief befalls the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	know that when blood flows from the artery, it may not be possible to heal it properly yourself even if the artery is large, unless one of the four methods we have mentioned is used:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cautery, or through extraction if it has not been treated, or by the tight binding of a thread, or with medicines applied that have the power to heal blood.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and bound and kept in place.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the tying or binding with cloths tightly or by putting heat-bearing things thereon, or other similar actions, if it doesn't prove effective.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they have no medicine present, then they should place their finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it out until the skin is completely healed above the wound and above the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And do not let it move, but moisten it with cold water often that it is very cold until the ice stays and grows and remains frozen;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make incisions in advance for those who need cauterization and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of treatments for amputations
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases for which fire cautery or burning medicines are required, and we discuss their uses, causes, instruments, and forms of cautery.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have covered this chapter up to the elbow, and I will proceed with this chapter in the same manner for what is found more easily and what you desire.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And when I begin this, it is important for you to understand that in this chapter there is more risk and fear than in the first section about using cautery, and for this reason, greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often evacuation of blood when opening veins, and incisions over abscesses, and treatments for wounds, and removals of arrows, and cuts into stones, and similar matters;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come to treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If they come from those who so suffered with their illness that they died lightly due to the anxiety they found in their sickness, and the severity of their disease;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And out of this comes fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And from these it is that you give its meaning, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am a bear";
et li maladie est despitouse.	And the illness is frustrating.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not right that you agree to those who come to you in this manner, but place more restraint on your honor than on your greed, and do not open rashly but wisely about what you are certain of, and for which you can take and leave.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And use diagnosis and guidance in your treatments for your illnesses where health may be transformed.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you gain good reputation, glory, and long-lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, our lords give you good understanding and justice, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of their hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have instructed this chapter according to its chapters, following what is before it in the section on cauteries, which I have outlined from the head down to the feet because you will find them more easily than those you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	From the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes from the child being born in childbirth, and when the mother holds the head of the child too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And never does it come about due to an unknown cause that we know not.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease occur in anyone other than children, and among all those that I have seen, it hastened their death;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And because of this, it seems to me that I should break off the work in parts of the treatment.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw that the child of him, the shoulder was full of water, and the head swelled each day until it could no longer be borne;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	And so much moisture had built up that he died, and this moisture was collected around the bone near the shoulder blade, between the body and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	And the operations are like this: when moisture is between the body and bone, and the abscesses are small that you cut through the head with a wide slit;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	And it should be as long as two of our fingers, so that the moisture can flow out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and this is how the pus looks:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, make two openings in a manner like a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is around the bone, and you see the edges of the head opening from every part, and when you press it with your hand internally, there's a sharp pain that doesn't stop:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If you must split through the head's middle, three cuts are necessary in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After binding the incisions with cloths and powders, then I put wine and oil, and leave it like this until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then remove the dressing and treat the wound with tents and treatments, and let the head heal evenly, then give the patient dry meat from a pig of water until the limb is strong and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is that you look at or expose the opening of the abscess, and join with water;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for it does not always present itself;
aucune fois derrier;	nor is it behind every time;
aucune fois en destre;	None of these times to the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and none of these times to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Therefore measure the cut or the incision, and fill with water, and do it according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and allow a flow of blood, so that the patient dies from bleeding and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of cautery by fire, command to the unwell that they let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When there occurs a disease which is called "catarrh" to the eyes or at the bottom (of the body), and the disease is old, and the treatment with medicine doesn't help, then the last resort of treatment could be cautery using what one would cauterize their two major arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, as soon as you see them cut, the patient should bleed after its head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After rubbing the injured area with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then pull the patient's neck to all parts of the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the veins are located, and where the hands of each are after the ears, and that's how they're positioned;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the hands of an eagle, and cut both of them with a sharp knife for two parts, as long as the vein extends to the bone, and do this along the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it, stop the bleeding from beneath the artery and above the cut, by making a cut also like one inch through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let the blood flow out continuously from up top.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open upon feeling it, you should measure the length of the space to three inches, then cut deeply into the eagle and proceed up to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And what needs to be removed of the blood is six cubic centimeters, and by chance slightly more or less, depending on how the patient can endure it, and the filling of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains on the bone tip of the spur, cut off the abscesses if none are found. Then suture and bandage the wound, and apply ointment treatment until it heals.
de emigrainne	Of the removal
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old age comes, and acute cough, because of the moisture from tears and heat in the temples and lower back that is beyond endurance and similar things. Medicine is treated with ways of medicinal cures and all this does not help him, so we extract the arteries in the temples and cauterize them, as we have reported.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is that the patient feels behind their temples and listens for the artery that emerges at the temple, because it opens well through its beating, and has little response beyond in some people who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is responsive, then suture the patient's neck with some cloths, then rub their head with a coarse cloth, and submerge their head in hot water until the artery appears clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatula with which this form is made:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Start by lightly scraping the skin until you feel the artery, then guide it upwards with forceps, and carefully remove all the tissues that are under each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is delicate, guide it to the tip of the distal phalanx, then cut that portion according to the size of both fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it isn't cut, or jumps not all at once,
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And let blood flow from six cuts, until three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, it's necessary that you tie it in two loops with a strong double silk thread, to prevent infection before the healing of the wound, and also to prevent continuous bleeding;
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then trim the excess that is between the two threads at that moment. And if you see fit, then cauterize with a surgical cautery until it reaches the bone as long as the shoulder head is trimmed;
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is a surgical procedure, if the patient doesn't have fever and has warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cautery helps to finish off moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	because it is of greater help against moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	It is necessary for the extraction of arteries where you fill up half of old cotton and place it under well-made tents;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are released, if you apply dry medicine substances that produce heat and tents until it is healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if you are uncertain about the location of the artery as far as your skill allows, use caution by fire, or fill the area with vinegar and squeeze it with your hand until the skin is tightened;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you do not have this tool at hand, you should immerse your arm up to the elbow in cold water until the ice melts, and lift it from cold water continuously while holding it as necessary;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And the one who is slippery and more easily extracted from the artery, you should cauterize the vein with this tool by cutting it in two parts, but make sure the cuts are well spaced to retain heat for longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too tight, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be about half a finger's width of space between the two knives. And when you signal to continue with the two of them, and place the hot iron until it reaches the bone, then cut the vein into two parts;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	And keep them apart on the shoulders because there is no welding with this cauterizer across the entire length;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes are draining from the veins that are above the test of the head's neck, and no cure with medicine works there, then you see the face of the patient turn red, and feel or perceive on their forehead as if they were trembling;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	And wherever they are touched and moistened so that the paper hairs fall, and the papers heat up, and are scorched by the heat of the tears, there is need for this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they called the old "treatment for burns", and when you do it again to the patient who has this illness, have hairs on their forehead, then make three cuts evenly across the forehead according to its length;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	And let one of the slits also like two all around on your forehead when swallowing down until near the nose, and the others two under the ribs by over the papers, and beware of the incisions of the arteries which are under the ribs by over the papers;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	And keep your hand away from the continuation of the two jaws, and let each wound have the size of three doves crossing paths;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And have an applicator of a sponge and cloth to dab it so as to wipe the blood, then pour the sharp spatula from two parts in which its form is made:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	From the incision that is behind the temple up to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	And scrape off all the keratin between the two slits across the entire surface of the skin that is on the bone, then make another incision from half way through the middle incision up to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	if you ignite in the first gap the tool called 'cultellaire', and it is very sharp on one side, but blunt on the other, it has this shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And make the cut towards the fatty part of the meat at the bone, and the cut should go towards the bone from the flesh, and stop when it feels halfway through the skin.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And take all the vessels that descend from the head with their eyes until the incision is continuous up to where it opens on the wound, and then proceed elsewhere in the middle crack up to the other end;
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	Then remove blood evenly, and express the wound for the contained blood;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	Then place a piece of old cotton in each crack, and lay wet cloths with wine, oil, and asphodel over them; make sure no pus remains.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And on the third day remove the bandage, and apply great plantations of tepid water, then administer a balm with basil oil and other treatments for wounds, until it heals.
dou reume des eulz	of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When there is no usual cough and you see the eyes become red and small, and weaken vision, and burned papers;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	And the hair grows, and one feels pain to fever, and the patient sweats.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	Therefore, know that these occurrences show that those matters and this putrid fluid come from many veins, and the wet treatment that it is, if is such.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you instruct the patient behind their forehead, then make a large cut in the middle of the forehead, and another one somewhat wide below this.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And begin from the left temple groove to the right temple, and make the incision up to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move with chewing;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	And when the bone is revealed, let all the blood drain onto an sponge, and then dress between the two edges of the cut, placing old cotton and linen;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then cover with wrappings moistened in wine and oil, and guard against pus formation;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	When it is being extracted, it must be that you rub the bone until the blood begins to emerge, then it is treated with excitative things, which make blood emerge.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of wheat flower, and four parts of comfrey, and make them into a plaster;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and apply this to the wounds to promote blood flow everywhere.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	From ear piercing
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everything that has an effect on ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	it could be grains, or an animal, or rock from mining, or something similar like iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seeds, such as beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or anything that flows, like water and oil, and similar substances.

S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it jumps out by means of forceps, that's good;

puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	Then press the glue onto the stone or whatever it may be, and proceed with force.

et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Continue the treatment as long as it is effective.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there are grains and they swell up, administer an extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it cannot come out, perform the puncturing with care according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision on that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not undertake this when you believe that the grains are damp due to ear moisture, until you have done many pieces of work;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then apply gentle pinching and suction, just as we have said, so that the extractions are done smoothly.

s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If she jumps for heaven, it's good.

puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then do it again with other sticks until all the sharp end comes out, as we have said about stones.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of the bug, if it is of small size like a mite and similar things, treat it as we have said in the division;

de l’estoupement des oreilles	From ear piercing
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without any wax in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	The same thing happens to adults through the impact of wounds or a fetus being born inside the ear. These impacts often enter the ear uncontrollably, unless one can see them;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	And never does the liquid overflow the wax, and it is seen clearly.
