de la char des papieres	From the page's contents
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This should be done each day when the eyes are moist and then dry. It is necessary to spread them with forceps and tweezers, and scrape the root of a snail's shell;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then place sulfuric acid powder on it.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if you cannot remove it by scraping, then apply a delicate round-hot iron for the cautery, and the cautery operator should perform an incision afterward.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	And many times they return, yet nothing remains from their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And when they are cauterized by fire, those roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	Of the gravel
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times, in papers, come things that seem to be gravel by their shape and hardness, and because of this is this disease called 'granuloma', and it is a gathering of thick moisture on the surface and beneath in the paper.
li ovraiges est telz:	The procedures are as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take care so that the granuloma does not move on one or both sides, and it is a simple matter to know this;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Stretch out first from a large area, then lightly cauterize each part, followed by pinching and pressing it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you cannot cover it without piercing the paper a little, but do not harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	And if there's a large tear, join it with stitches, and treat until it heals properly;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	And if it's small, don't apply too much force, because the ointment will quickly restore and grow new flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if it's large and descending into the ear towards the upper part, invert the paper, place the granule on needles, apply them from one side to the other;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	And if the paper is moved by the incision, it does not harm anything.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	And when the large ice has been broken, remove the salt water eye, and cleanse the place from that which infects flesh until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the granulomas
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a type of fat that is found in the weaves of paper sheets and this happens more often among children than adults. It causes much trouble for their eyes, and it comes to them at dawn, and they cannot look at the sunlight because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And because of this, they lie down on their faces for a long time, and sleep on them, and have the paper sheets under their eyes wet from sweat that causes puffiness and an appearance over them due to the Exinach which opens in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press on the arm with your fingers and feel the pulse between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the way of treating it is that the patient puts their head in your healthy state;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	And then take a linen sheet, and prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the amount that escapes from each part, then place it on him;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	And press with your thumbs on both sides, so that the escape is gathered within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	Then in the middle of the moisture on the skin, cut a slit about as wide, and not more than the wound one makes in the cleansing of veins;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	And let the skin be in place until you see the escape.
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	And from many dispositions comes escape from the slit, according to the shape of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Remove then with one piece of cloth between your thumbs at the back, and turn your hand to the right and left until it disperses;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And ensure you do not adjust within the fissure, that you do not reach the entire spleen up to the eye, that you do not pierce it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if they emerge not at the beginning of the fissure, then widen it gently until it opens;
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then pull it out as we have said, then moisten it with oil and water, and place it on the head, and stretch it with bands.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are such individuals who grind salt and place it to corrupt the moisture that remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the doctor should treat as long as they remain healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if pus starts to form in the arm, so the doctor uses plasters that soothe until they remain healthy.
des poilz des papieres	The phrase "des poilz des papieres" translates directly to "the hairs of papers". This might refer to paper fibers or could be metaphorical depending on context. Without more information, this is the literal translation.
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hair that is not naturally born appears and ages, if it harms the eyes, they can lead to diseases like habitual watering of the eyes and degeneration of the papers (possible typo) and impotence, all of which can be a cause of eye damage;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment follows four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	Using a fire cautery, using medicine according to what is described in the previous chapter on cautery, and doing it through cutting and stitching or by ligature, as I will explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary that you place the head of the ear in your health, then turn the paper of the eye to your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If it has turned, it is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, then insert a needle through all the threads;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and whether that goes across the edge of the paper where the hair grows beneath these hairs, and pull the thread upwards through all the paper, and then trim it with scissors;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then do it in the part under the paper, under the closely fitted hairs, all across the nostril opening, from the large tear to the small;
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then extract the thread, and place on the paper a small cotton ball and gauze tent, then mark on the paper an oak leaf shape, similar to the bay leaf, and always ensure that the figure matches the amount you see when lifting the paper which is placed underneath.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if at that time it has need for handling paper of large quantity according to how the paper is softened;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then make along all the veins above the two lines you have marked, and start with large drops until small ones;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	Let it be one of the splits near the natural hairs in growth as large as a root, then place the comfrey at one of the two corners on that side, then scrape thoroughly.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	Then gather the two lips together using a needle with all one thread of fine wool. Clean out the blood, and remove excess thread on the two corners at any sticky areas. If you see fit to do this;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	And if that doesn't suit, if you don't mind it, then leave the stitches and threads for up to three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then cleanse the wound without using wet or sticking materials, for paper burns upon contact with the wound and its assembly, but the stitches rot (as the old ones said), and it is work without fear;
et si a une autre maniere:	And if there's another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	And if you want to cut paper into a shape that is as round as the leaf of myrtle, like we have told, in three inches square according to the form shown here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then take what stands above the smaller forces evenly according to the shape which is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you do not have the ability to hold the forceps, and the thing is not equal, then take a needle or where there is thread, and stick it through at the tip;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and pierce another thread through the large artery, and the second thread through the small one, and join the threads evenly between your fingers;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin over which you have incised, just like we have described, then join the two edges of the wound with stitches, and treat it until it is healed;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if pus comes to your incision, soothe it with tallow and similar soothing ointments;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes the hair of the paper gets converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	It is necessary for you to use what we have instructed about incisions;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the suturing in one and the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment for scabies follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and you should cut the paper and make an incision according to what I have said, then create two canals by hand, and also sew two fine threads as long as the paper and as wide as the needle is;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and tie each of the two ends with one of the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then delicately join the two at what is above the paper of the eye, and tighten the two canals from each part forming;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	And let it remain for a few days, and the skin which is restricted will die and decay, until it escapes through itself.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it drags on, if the condition persists with strength, then treat him as long as he remains sound;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound is healed, and if it lifts the paper, and no more hair will grow;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of two cauldrons that you will make according to this diagram, and according to this size in length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The operations are such that you take a fine needle and thread it with silk string and it is strong and fine;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then join the ends together and tie them finely, and let the length of the threads be half a palm in length;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then arrange for the hunt another fine silk thread briefly, and tie the knot of the thread.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then place the patient's eye on healthy part;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And let the sun down so that the works are clear, for it's an intricate and small work. Then fix the needle all through the hunt in the root of the well-adjusted hair, and pierce on the paper quickly as you pull it above the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then remove the hair up to the hunt, and fix that hair in the hunt if there is one, two, three or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then remove your hand until the hairs remain out all through the paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the chase (presumably referring to hunting or tracking) has been treated and the hairs do not grow with it, then pull the chase away from the wound up until you ordered it to be placed, as long as the chase feels forceful downwards and when you see this through your eye's vision;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Therefore, pull the chase and the thread, and cover the eye and leave it covered for two or three days, as long as the hair grows in its place and the flesh starts to grow.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are small, then accompany with one long hair as found naturally on a cow, and raise it along with whatever you leave or allow to remain, until it is lengthened, then raise it.
de la porriture de l’oil	Regarding eye infections
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease which is called "aleacrati" or eye putrefaction occurs in the eye, if there are two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One is natural, and the other is unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And happens suddenly due to an injury or surgery, or from similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way to work on it is that you split this seam and open the lips of it, and put linen cloths inside, and bind it until it's healed;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And it is not right for you to use in its treatment things that dry out and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the sickness will return worse than the first one;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but use things that soften, such as fennel;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	And let it be rinsed with hot water or oil and linseed oil, and apply garlic poultices in none of the oils, and wrap it in a cloth, and treat it with this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the treasures of your treatment are that you must beware so that it does not join without regard to its former shape;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And the remedies that we have described do not exclude directions for this illness, so that it does not recur according to its former form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	Of the matter that comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease, which truly is called 'dislocation', and it is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	Accidents arise from wounds, tears, cauterizations, and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And in executing the procedure for this you take a needle with two threads, insert it into the flesh, and make it pierce from the left eyelid to the right eye socket so that the thread passes through two parts of the flesh.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then the flesh is stretched above all the needle, and it cuts across the wide space of the spatula.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the figure on the paper returns according to what is appropriate, it's good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	And if not, then take a ruler and place it in the groove, turn the paper, and cut two grooves where they would have been inside the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	Let the ends of the two grooves at the two corners of the cut you made be arranged, and make an angle such that when they are assembled, the figure is as that of a letter which forms a 'G' in Greek;
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then shape that flesh according to the size and thickness of its edges as they were before, based on where the paper was, then align the two needed parts, and stitch with a thread like yarn;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then follow the treatment we have discussed for softening medicines and ointments, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease originates from a cut or stitch or cauterization, it is necessary that you make an incision full of hair along the lines of the hair on the skin, and according to what was mentioned before;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then sew between the two leather panels of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and you should perform the operation according to the shape of the disease, for it is very diverse in shape, and the skilled surgeons prepare all kinds of tools so they can return the form to its natural state;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and even for patients themselves, according to what needs treatment and the use of various tools in multiple configurations.
dou soudement de la papiere	right along the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this bonding occurs in a manner between hands where the paper above is bound with the white of the oil and cannot move or perform its natural operations, then it is necessary that you bind the tip of a razor under the paper, and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	And extend with the pincers, until you hold what is disturbed under the delicate point of the cautery, which must neither be too hot nor too sharp, so that the patient does not suffer from the heat being too intense and scorching their eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	And make your cut, from which you sear that united one lightly, so that the skin heals according to its natural form;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	And heal the whole united part, and do not perform any sharp operation in the eye, and use sweet water for washing, and wear a collar;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	Then place between the skin and the eye a linen tent, and put wet wool from an egg over the eye;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	And after three days use hot water and other warm things until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	From the edge of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that the nail follows two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	It is nervous and appears like hard leather, and another that is not nerveless but appears like white moisture frozen, such that when you touch it with iron and treat it using hot needles, if it doesn't hurt.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	Both of them begin near the large tear duct, and grow slowly, slowly until they cover all the eye and all the light and the movement of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incision is that the patient places their head in your healthy position, then you operate on their eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and lift the paper with your hand, then bend the nail with small hot needles, and extend it above;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and I put horse hair, or cow hair, or bull hair, and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the needle point slightly and insert it into the nail, then pierce through the entire length of the needle, attaching the nail with a thread and extending it above, then scrape off all hair from the base of the nail that is under the cuticle and up to the hair at the base of each hair follicle and skin, leaving the natural tear by the tears so that upon incision there is no usual body discharge;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	Each time you extend only the nail to the cuticle alone, and with the thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then scrape off all hair from this area: it is the form:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And ensure that the splinters do not touch the fatty tissue and break it, and that the thorns do not pierce.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	And after the incision pour some of the pus in the eye, and make a spoon from silver, and leaves it until another day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat as needed so long as they are well.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not made of bone, and you cannot push in the needle, and the crescents cannot enter it, this condition is treated many times with medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	And it grows in the way I have described in the division; and if you see it swell, this creates an eye problem from a disease, and take the splinter lightly sharp according to this shape:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And remove the nail gently upwards, and if you see that it does not diminish at all and your reason presses on, then drip from your mouth into a ring-like eye made of stannic oxide and red and white amalgamated, and bathe the eye until another day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then repeat the other operation according to this same procedure, until everything is excavated.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If there is nothing against your vision, like pus-filled blisters, then you should proceed, and first treat the pus-filled blister until it's cleansed, then restart the procedure as described previously, until it's cleansed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the tissue from the lacrimal gland causes harm in the eye at night, then suspend it with honey, and take only part of it and not all, so that no tears may come;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then drip into the red eye ring which is made of stannic oxide.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows around the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	There are some people who do not grow red eyes, and cover the pupil, restraining on papers and turning outside, and seem like a candle flame;
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the operations are such that when one's body heals its head, then it opens the eyes, and all of that flesh to an extent suitable for this, and supports it with strength;
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then remove the first layer of flesh, and carefully shave it all until the end, and ensure you do not irritate the eye during the operation.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision be gentle as we described in the section about nail incisions and using small forces with it, just like the form shown after this chapter's demonstration.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the incision is completed and all flesh has been removed, apply oil of sulfur or distill a red colander and similar corrosive medicines on it. Place cotton soaked in egg white over this to protect against pus; make sure there's no open wound that could cause infection.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	And if it remains motionless, and the patient sweats profusely, and you suspect an abscess at the spot, then let your eye observe and treat the abscess with soothing remedies.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work as long as it is safe, and thus make four cuts and join them together in the eye according to this manner.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But nevertheless, it must be that you adapt the treatment of each natural weakness in the eye;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and of the accidental path through which a metal object has passed;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	And do not leave your hand in any of these incisions until you see that this limb endures the cut.
des voines des eulz	of veins and eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	When the veins are red that cover over the eye, and cause harm to sight for days.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	So then the task of the first one is to look at where the eye is, and if it's dislodged, or outwards, and there is no other disease besides the dislodgement;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Therefore correct this as follows:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to place their head in a healthy position, then suspend all those veins according to their wisdom for as long as possible. And make sure that each pulse is doubled according to this shape:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be two inches by degree on one side according to this shape:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then work on these veins subtly, and see the blood flow hour after another, until you see those veins being removed from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And make sure you don't burn the eye at the ends of the spatumiles, and do this operation at midday in front of the sun, and be very zealous in your work so that you only handle those veins;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, if you distill into the eye a collar of green and red for to corrupt that which remains under the inflammation.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you do not have the strength to perform this all in one go, make a plaster with things that soothe the pain from the eyes and leave it on for some days until the pain is soothed and there's assurance of no abscess formation, then continue according to this method as described until recovery occurs;
et c’est li forme des forces:	And these are the forms of strength:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the duct of the eye
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The wound is called "arissati" in this context:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you treat it using cautery and hot medicine as I have described previously, and if it does not heal, there is a place within the wound where an abscess forms, near what should be its point of entry. Remove all the moisture that's there, until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when you uncover the bone, and you will see the corruption and the darkness, if you take all of the instrument that is formed here;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	And it is called 'hard leader', and may be made of steel indented at the tip, and should be pointed like a file as it is in this present shape:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place on it the tip of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your fingers, and press your hand a bit until you know that that corruption has been removed;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	And do this once, then restore the head of medication-drying.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the joints are joined, and scar forms, and the body of the bone is joined, and remains like this for 40 days, and does not heal and does not become pus-filled, and no bad incidents happen, you know that it is healed;
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, if there is no other organ except to bring the sinus back into its place according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	And when you uncover the bone for the second time with a metal tool and by using aqueous medicines; and if it has been uncovered then take your axe according to this form, and secure the piece of iron with three angles, and let the handle be thin until as far as you see depicted here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place it against the bone near the eye socket, and keep your hand away from your eye just slightly, then turn your axe until it pierces the bone and you feel the pain in your ear as long as your hand is on your nose;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	Then restore the area with dry medicines as I have instructed, and when the heat starts and hardens your hands, take the material to your nose;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	If something is lighter for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	From the exit of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eyes open completely everywhere, and there is no disturbance in the heart or diminishment, it is necessary that you bind the patient;
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then heal him, then apply suction cups or bandages without piercing to evacuate it, then place over the eye I a bandage made of acacia and aloe and incense and gallows flesh, and then release the eye, and plaster it with strips and cloths;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And the method of the cloths is that you take cloths sufficiently soft, and fold each one into four, and then place one on top of another according to the amount that the eye needs;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	Then apply by means of a hard binding above, and reapply the suction cups to evacuate without piercing;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	Then apply the suction cups and keep the eye restrained day and night, and if it starts to close, you must keep it closed.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	Then loosen the bandage after day and night, and if you see the eye heal, that's good;
se ce non;	If not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	if you have to re-wrap, bandage, and apply the eye patch along with the bandage and suction cups until it is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	At the rupture of the ovarian membrane
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruptions come in the vitreous thread, then open and comes out force of paper like resin bits, and it is observable;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	Therefore, if you see it covered, the operation is like poking an awl into the root of half above the lower part, then poke another awl where there is doubled thread at the tear part;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	And make a puncture, and let the first needle according to its placement;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then place a loop of the thread double and tie part of the eyelid from inside outwards, then tighten it well. After that, remove the needle and place a wet wool on the eye with plenty of egg mixture;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and let it be until the thread has healed with the eyelid; then treat the eye with comforting substances until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and afterwards, each part of the wound is held in place by one half of a circular piece of cloth until it has healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eyes do show a prominent appearance, then puncture through the thin membrane that comes under the eye, and dry out the moist pus and allow the eyes to sink in quickly.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Take out as long as it remains healthy.
de la bowe de l’oil	Of the oil of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called 'alcunnati' can only be found in bile that has gathered in the gallbladder, resembling a pointy object descending, and it is not an actual needle;
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the way to observe this process is that you make the patient sit on the operation table and have them face forward straightly. Then hold their head with both hands at two points, and move it until you see the needle coming above your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then either place it there and keep it from going down until the light is gone, and see how things are happening as they should;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	And if it doesn't descend anywhere, know that it is a needle, and when the descent of the needle isn't as we have described.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	If you make the patient sit between your hands, then take the fine spatula and perform on the corneal surface an incision from point I to the continuation of the conjunctiva with the corneal tissue and the crown, until the blood flows;
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when it has flowed out, if you distill it into the eye with hot water mixed with honey, or hot water with boiled fenugreek and honey, then apply other remedies until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	Of the waters of the eye
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have the appearances of the waters in the division, and what needs to be pierced;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	if done according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary that you place the patient between your crossed hands, away from the light towards the sun, and tie the healthy eye tightly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then place the paper of the eye on your left hand where the eyes are on the left, or on your right hand where the eyes are on the right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, where the eyes are on the left, the tool that is called 'almagda', or in your left hand, where the eyes are on the right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the tool beneath the cornea at the thickness of an eyelash in that corner of the eye to the part below the minor tear duct, then force the tool called 'almagda' vigorously, and turn your hand until it pierces through the corner of the eye, and feel when almagda reaches the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it must be that the size of the almagda's passage matches the size of the space from the cornea to the edge of darkness.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	And this is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	You will see the bone inside through the transparency of the cornea paper, and then place the tool until it reaches where the tip is, then express out one after another along a path.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	Let the patient now see his illness before him and the instrument in their mind.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After laying him down, and if the tip rises up to the second path, apply force with the tool, and when it is securely in place and no longer ascends, gently remove the wax by turning your hand back and forth.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	And then place a small amount of beryl in the water, and remove the eye from inside it.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then place the oiled or greased eye shutters or wool soaked in rose oil and a plenty of eggs, and bind it with a healthy oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	Yes, and those that belong to our time should be placed on the common broth with plenty of eggs.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if almagda cannot enter the eye because of its hardness, as there are some people whose eyes are too hard, it is necessary for you to take the tool called "alberit," which has this form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And therefore pierce only the conjunctiva, do not go too far around it, but make it subtle. Then pour out the wax, as we have said;
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	And upon completion of his work, the surgeon, accompanying the patient, instructs him to sleep on his back in his dark room;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	And avoid all movements, and please eat light meats, and do not move your head to the right or left. Secure him accordingly until half of the day;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then release him in that dark house itself, and test his vision. Make him see nothing, then reapply the bandage until seven days;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	And it is not advisable for you to do this during the treatment or after incision now. Instead, apply this method because the wound has swollen rapidly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	When it comes to discharging pus, you should release the eye before the seventh day and apply treatment to him who relieves pus.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when they are calmed down, open the eye and place an ointment on its lid for a few days to cover it, and be in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then leaves the house little by little, and transforms into its place;
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	Know that no one should intervene in such cases.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us who was from the Iberian Peninsula, who told us that there they used a type of garlic called "almagda," which one bathed in water, but still we have never seen any such thing in our land, nor have I ever read about it in old books;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And by chance, this is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of almond shapes, because those who do not know them see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and be of good arane properly:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	And indeed the head of such from this same subtlety, and the rear end in three angular pains.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh around the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	No birth or creature is made from various connected fleshes, some of which appear to be scorpions with the legs of a bird;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	And if there are such creatures or one has flesh with dark color and if there is flesh with good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	From those creatures that have good color and not dark, it is necessary for you to place the patient between your hands facing the sun;

And if it's malignant ulcers, if you act quickly and cauterize as long as the wound is bleeding and all the muscles are cooked through, then pour or flush it with cold water or wine.

adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Therefore it is necessary that you insert a thread of linen somewhat thick, and have your hands tied together, and there should be between each knot the space of an inch or less;

puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	then hold the head that comes through the nose with one hand, and the other head that comes out of the mouth with the other hand, and know them one after another while being guided by us who are holding the thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you know that the thread has corroded that flesh, then pull out the thread, drain the blood, moisturize the thread with Egyptian ointment, and quickly return it to its place at the nose as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Make it for three days or more, until the ointment dissolves all that is buried in flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	And then apply or inhale a row of opium for several days until it heals, and if there is need for dried medicine substances, use them accordingly.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the tool for purging the head, with which one distills oils and medicines or inhales them:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And whether it's made of silver or arsenic, resembling an open lamp or like a cane, guide it in the same manner;
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	And if you see fit, make a closed cane, and ensure the tools are full for purging the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	And have your hand ready above the head to hold when one heats the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh around the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a disease is born at the nose which is called 'Toul', it grows and becomes large until it reaches something to be seen.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And thus it is necessary that you start by covering it up, and let the bone fully heal, then place your cauterizing tool or hot medicine.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	And if you delay covering it when it is large, take heed if it's hard, if it changes color, if it shows poor sensation:

And if the abscess is due to heat rather than change in color, and you see that it can be completely covered, let the patient drain and cover without fear, and treat with dry and restraining remedies.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the nose is cut and stitched
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when solutions for prolongation come into contact with one of these venous loops, it benefits little, because in some people.

ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	by needles, as we have said about the stitch for the belly;

des apostemes des levres	from abscesses of the lips

de la char des gencives	from the flesh of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times there grows on the gums a grayish deposit that the old call "albula";

si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	if it does not return after the cautery;

des sordens	Of cauteries with fire command the sick person to let the hairs grow long and evenly; if they pierce at their root, hold the eyes firmly so they don't move until they fully grow.
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	They are gathered at the root of the teeth, inside the mouth between the gums, and they consist of ugly and hard scabs;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	And in no instance do you find black and yellow teeth with worms, until the decay reaches the gum, and the teeth smell;
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	If it is necessary for you to have the sick person sit between your hands, and his head be in its proper place, and touch both teeth or skin until there is nothing remaining.

et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	And if you remove what is at the primary cause, it's good;
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	But if not, begin again on the second day and the third, until you have taken everything;
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	Know that teeth require various types of instruments to be extracted, according to what the work demonstrates, because the remover used for taking out teeth at the surface has other shapes than those used between the teeth;
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	And these forms and others are equipped with you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary when you treat the tooth's pain that you delay the extraction for as long as possible, because it should not cause any harm.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because this is such an intense substance that one would not have any excuse for scratching it.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	So when the patient is constrained to bleed, it's necessary for you to know exactly where to puncture.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain moves through the body, and beware if it's toothache or a disease of the teeth, then extract the good tooth;
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	and still do not leave the pain alone until the bad tooth is removed, for we have already wanted to do this for our soldiers;
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are certain of the tooth that hurts, it is necessary to incise around the tooth all the way through two or three millimeters to keep the gum from spreading in every direction;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then guide it to your hands or with the use of delicate forceps at each poke and poke, until they are well dislocated, then firmly secure the forceps.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and have the shoulder of the patient between your knees, and keep it steady so that it doesn't move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the right tooth straight without breaking it, and if it doesn't spring back, take none of these instruments and insert them gently into each half, and move it like you did first.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if there is a hole and you can feel it, then it's necessary to fill it with cloths, where the holes are;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if you squeeze gently with the forceps, so that it doesn't break while squeezing.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And it must be quite carefully open in the gum to remove the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And be sure to handle it well so you don't break it, and if any part remains, inform the patient of the greater pains caused by the remnants of the root after the initial extraction.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware that you do not do as the ignorant surgeons do, who break the bone every time out of their haste and boldness, and they do not bring to completion what we have told.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	But one comes with each time by the action of this great disease through the roots that they endure, or through the matter that they break, as we often wish;
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the tooth is extracted, wash the socket with wine or brandy and vinegar;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	And if there is bleeding which often occurs, when treating it, fill the socket with powdered vitriol;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	And if that doesn't work, apply cautery to it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The forms of the tools by which you first remove teeth should have long points and thick handles, such that they do not bend when you are pulling out teeth;
et ce sont les formes:	and these are their forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And may have large limbs that do not bend while being used, and be made of strong iron well-crafted, with teeth for gripping.
de la racine des dens	from the roots of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root stays during the extraction, it is necessary to put in the socket wet cotton soaked with butter for a day or two until the joints are softened. Then take out the forceps which are called 'algefri', as the patient seems to require care.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	And be sure that they are done as with a file and it is this shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out completely with these pliers, it is necessary that you uncover the entire flesh up to the root, and place the instrument known as "althali," which means palmache, as it is formed thus:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And be sure to make them strong and thick so that they do not break at all, and if the root jumps over this, it is good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If not, assist with all the instruments from which the forms come next:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if help is taken from this tool which has two points, as it is formed thus:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other tools that are in front according to the size of teeth, and this tool which seems like large pliers, as it is formed thus:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And be sure that these instruments do not break and know that many instruments from the socket exist;
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	And also other instruments, which are not even mentioned;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	And the wise surgeons find their tool by themselves, according to what their works and diseases show them. For there are some illnesses where the old did not teach any tool because of the diversity among these, or when it breaks part of the bone or from others, or it decays, if they search for the tools that suit, as I have said, and help with gestures, which is described here, concerning this form:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And let them be thick and well gripping to hold the bone, so it doesn't slip but can be held and removed;
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	And then restore the area with suitable medicines for this, and if there's decay in the bone and it is small, take it all with this tool:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears not according to its natural course, and its form is ugly, even especially in virgins, you should know that it has been born after the tooth, and isn't properly placed, and one cannot take care of or sharpen it.
adonques lou raie;	therefore the fold;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	and if it is in line with the tooth, take this tool as described, and let its shape resemble that of a small beak, and make it from iron that stays sharp.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the tooth is ground slowly with my hands day by day due to the hardness of its root, and because you do not move the others, and if it appears that one can be filed, then I file it in a single piece like this:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and is also like the awl's file that one uses to make needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and carefully file the tooth a little bit by bit with your hands gently, until it doesn't move as long as you continue;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	then in the end smooth it off with a scraper, and if the tooth is too sharp and hurts the tongue, you should file down the roughness until it's even, so as not to hurt the tongue or impair speech.
quant li dent lochent	when the tooth rots
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When it comes to the front tooth or by tapping or striking, and if a patient cannot press on what they are eating that they do not defecate, and you have treated them with constrictive medicines, then this is ineffective.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	if they need to be restrained with an golden thread, for silver threads turn green and decay, but gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and let the thread neither be too thick nor too thin, according to the size of the gap between the teeth;
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you see to straighten the teeth, take the thread and hold both ends between the two healthy teeth, then place the dislocated tooth between the misaligned teeth, whether one or more, as long as you can feel it properly up to the healthy tooth on the other side;
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then resume the covering until you have reached the part where you stopped, and apply your hand skillfully and carefully, until it does not move at all.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and bind your floss to the tooth root so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then hold the teeth with forceps and join them together; place them between healthy teeth, making sure they do not irritate the tongue;
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and leave it like this as snugly as possible while still allowing movement, and if it dislodges or the string breaks, use another string to tighten it again;
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it allowed for movement and remained like this throughout its use, and that is the shape of the teeth and the position of the two healthy back teeth and the two front ones as you can see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the jaw is dislocated, if it is placed back in its position, repeatedly freshly, as we have said;
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and do not interfere with it unless you are cautious and endure pain, and no time is made in the shape of an ox bone tooth, and we place it where the defect is, and hold it steady as we have said, and remains and serves for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	covering the wound of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Not once is it possible for the strings that come from under the tongue or the jaw to form this way; we do not create such things.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by chance due to a healed wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the operations are such that you work on the mouth with the aid of medicine, have its head in your healthy position, and lift the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	Then connect the nervous cord across the wound, until the tongue is dislocated from its place, and if there is stiffness or swelling, and this is sudden injury, if you break the hook and reconnect it firmly;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	And make sure that the cut isn't too deep, for there is an artery underneath;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	And when you have done this, if you raise the wound to the pink water and cold air, or to cold water, then place a linen tent over the tongue;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	And treat it with herbs every night, so that the wounds do not heal incorrectly.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if there is blood leaking out, put vinegar over the wound.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if it does not stop bleeding, cauterize with the slow cautery, which is good for this purpose;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	Then follow another treatment as long as it is salutary,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	And if you see it is reddish or black or hard, even when the patient doesn't feel it and there's no touch to it, for it indicates a putrefaction;
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	And if it is decaying into phlegm, and there's moisture, then let the pus flow out, and make a fine incision, and discharge it from both sides;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	And if it doesn't taste good in your work, then put vinegar to boil until it's thoroughly infused, then return to your work as long as you're using the entire strength;
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift up the limb and the joint, and follow other treatments as long as it is beneficial.
des apostemes de la gorge	From throat abscesses
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	None of the time comes within the throat valves which are called 'godath', and they should be correctly known as the two almond shaped parts. And when you treat them, as we have stated in the division, if they remain unsanctified, take care:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If it's hard pus of small sense and with a woody texture, do not touch it with metal.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it's red and the root is large, don't touch it with metal either, for fear of bleeding.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	but leave it until it is healed, and then you will remove it, or it would burst on its own;
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it's whitish in color and the root is delicate, prepare your instrument properly but first check that the pus bubble rests and calms down.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	So have the patient sit in front of the sun, and his head should be upright, and let him open his mouth and hold the surgeon's knife between his hands, and press his tongue down until it meets the entire instrument, this is how it is done.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	And may be made of silver or finely crafted iron as sharp as knives:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	Can't you press the tongue to this entire instrument, and can you see the abscess? If so, take an ounce and pierce it into the almond, and force it upwards more than you can.
