Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The forms of the forces in universal transformation are as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Let both shoulders be held and cut, and let the shoulders also be as large as the arms equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error in universal transformation occurs when the kidneys flee during incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, it is necessary for you to extend until your nail, so that the legs perform an incision;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And do it evenly, and if you cannot hold it at your nail, then hold it with pliers, and then proceed.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they pierce through for three days, and the one who is beneath the member swells, you should let it be until the pus is calmed by exudation, and lightly scrape it.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And when you can endure it, protect the part of the member, for this will not harm him.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	So treat the burn of wounds with powder, as we have said or discussed about powders, and if you exceed due measure in heating it, and it goes beyond, it will not cause harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat accordingly, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	Regarding the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Retention of urine is due to the obstruction of stones, or blood that has frozen, or bile, or pus, or similar things, as we have discussed in the section;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the patient is not relieved of his urine, and you see that it is being held back by a stone in the bladder or neck of the bladder, then it's necessary for the patient to be raised on his knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And have his feet placed under the back, and extend his stomach from the part above the back, and hold the patient so that he cannot move until he can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And then the necks of the bladder must be forced to express the stone above, so that the urine is relieved.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it doesn't come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you should administer extraction with all the instrument that is called "syringe", which here is its form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And may it be fine silver strands of light hair, such as those of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And let it be the length of a palm and a half, and fine at its root.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And for the passage of urine, take a double thread and tie it around a small part of wool or cotton at its root, and keep the root inside the syringe with the thread.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And cut off the excess of the wool and keep it until the end of the syringe, then smear the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit down, and squeeze the bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and vinegar.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	And gently place the syringe in the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the anus.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Firstly, insert the syringe before reaching the bladder, and guide it until you feel the patient's urine coming to the empty thing; this does not follow the exact order as some might lead her in a twisted direction.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then pull the thread until all the wool is done little by little, and the urine follows the thread. Then pull it out, making sure to properly drain the urine.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And keep using the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and relieve the patient of their discomfort.
des maladies de la vessie	Of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood come into the bladder, or corruption is assembled there, and you see distilled waters and medicines, do so with all the instrument that is called "clepsydra", and it has this form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It's closed, and if it's been three attempts:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And let urine flow through where the medicinal cure should be such that it numbs the penis well without additional substances. If there is moisture to expel, allow it to flow out as needed; and push if necessary.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see your medications flowing into the bladder, place the end of the catheter in the moisture, and pull at the one who is attached.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	if you pull on the catheter at the other end, then firmly reconnect the catheter afterwards;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	if moisture enters from there, and goes to the bladder now, so that the patient feels it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of subtle colic in which one irrigates the bladder:
si est ci:	if it is like this:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And made of silver or horn, and the shoulder is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and downwards to the back or under the armpits;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with the moisture you use to irrigate the bladder. Then tie it between the two breasts in a good double thread, and heat one end of the moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Apply the blistering agent to the head of the bladder in the penis, then hold your hand over the bladder until all moisture accumulates there, as long as the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	And if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make it into a circle, piercing it roundly through.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then insert a strong thread into these pustules, then join the circle just as one would tie a knot, and put inside it what you see of pus, moisture, and water, and secure it with the tool.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	Do this just like you did with the bladder, squeezing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	from the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have discussed the methods of stone treatment and extraction together with remedies;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And I have explained the difference between a kidney stone that has been attacked by rain, and all the signs, and in which kidney one should open for size;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	And in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I will explain it clearly and succinctly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the kidney stone within the bladder usually occurs more often in children, and this is a sign that an infection has spread from the bladder similar to one that spreads subtly;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	And when it is in the urethra, and affects the urinary organs of the penis, and it passes many times, and then becomes hard;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and at the end of these infections, the kidneys
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is lighter until they are four years old, and there is much complaint in the elderly, and it's moderate for those between middle age and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the treatment is more gentle for those with large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient by purging, in order to extract all the pus that is inside.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it clogs up every time when trying to cut into the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take hold of the stone by its edges, and pull it out while moving downwards, so that the stone descends to the front of the bladder, and emerges only once from its upper part;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have him sit between your hands while preparing everything, and his hands under his thighs, so that the bladder is fully hanging downwards;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then seize it and feel inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you sense the stone in space, cut immediately on the stone now.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if she doesn't pass with the touch along all of it, wet your index finger of your left hand with urine, for if the stone is young, or with half your finger, for if the stone is a mature adult;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	And dig until you reach its base, aim for the stone, and when you feel it under your finger, if it touches the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press towards your finger, and dig further in the place where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the surgeon to press the bladder with his hand, and command him to spread upwards both legs with his right hand, and hold the skin that covers the legs with his left hand in the area where the cut will be made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then dig into the fatty tissue, which is its form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between what's in between the legs and the base, not in the middle but at the edge of the left side of the bladder;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And be straight on the stone, and your feet should lie on a base or foundation, and be made to span across it so that it is wide outside but narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	By chance if the press needed which is or foundation, that it may jump to make sense of work;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	And know that there are parts of stone where there are angles and edges:
si est griés a issir;	if it is torn to exit;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and if it is at parts that are under, resembling a walnut, and round, whose exit is light.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	And above where there are angles and edges, make the size larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	And if it does not jump, then you should tighten with the tongs that are like a file at their tip, to force out the stone so that it doesn't escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	for you thrust out of it with the slender curved instrument to the head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot work it like this, if it is large but quite small and rough, and if you do not debone it, then season it with vinegar;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, if you remove the largest first from the neck of the bladder, then cut upwards, then force out the tract, and afterwards the smaller ones if there are any.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if she is very large, then one must cut her out, and create a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	or he dies, or his urine comes out immediately even if his legs cannot be sewn together;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but strive nonetheless to pull or break it with forceps until you extract it piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And when you have finished your work, cleanse the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, then bind it. Place a moist cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and cold water and rosewater, to soothe the inflamed area.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then straighten the hair up on his neck, and do not loosen the tie until midday.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you untie it, be sure to raise the head and torso very well with oil and water, then wash with ointment of laudanum and ointment of basil until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if abscesses come into the wound and infections occur, or blood clots in the bladder, causing retention of urine, which is known to behave like this: without urination with the urine.
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	So then burn your tool in the wound, and remove that blood, because if it remains, it will corrode the bladder;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cleanse the wound from water and slime and pus, and assist with all methods that you know, until it is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And ensure that all the remedies you use, you bind his two legs together, and apply the remedies on the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if his stone is small and it's led by the penis, and stuck inside, causing inability to urinate;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	If you follow what I say as such, that you trim many times and excuse the loss of size due to this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already gained this experience.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one piece of iron according to this shape, and let there be three pegged points in it.
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take thread and bind around the penis near the stone, so that it cannot come back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then gently push the stick in the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	And turn the drill to your hand in the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	If it comes to an end quickly, then press your hand onto the one that is stuck of the stone which is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks soon, and jump with the urine, and the patient will be freed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie a thread over the stone and another on top, then place the penis between the two threads, then pull hard, and release one of the threads, and cleanse all the coagulated blood in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it as long as it is clean.
de la piere des femmes	From the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	A stone may become lodged inside a woman, and if it happens even once, the treatment is exhausting, and must be resisted for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason could be that perhaps the woman is still a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	And the second reason is that it might be difficult to find a woman who would willingly reveal her condition under scrutiny, especially if she is pure.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third way could be that perhaps it might be hard to find a woman who knows this art well;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth way is that perhaps the stone in a woman's body might be deeper than in men's, so it requires deeper cutting; and there is great fear involved. If you must resort to this, then seek out someone very skilled for this task, and guide her hand well; if you can't find such a person, you might not dare let a pure person look into this matter further.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And there comes a clear insight into the life of women, where a woman who understands some part of the art is instructed and commanded to do what you command concerning the inquiry of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	And carefully observe whether that woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	Then it must be pushed with force or at the very least seek out the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And if she finds it, force her with due measure and seek the stone, and I advise that she push her effort or press against her hand on the bladder's formation with her left hand and presses firmly.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	And if she finds it, it is necessary for her to move it gradually from the entry of the bladder until beneath, as far as she can reach the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut on the stone at the root of the thigh over the middle of the femur, where you can see the bone, and feel the bone in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his tool above the stone or nearby it, but make him small at the beginning.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then pinch the vein at the opening, if you feel the bone increase the wound as much as the bone can be forced out, and know that many types of stones are:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	which means, small and large, hard and smooth, long and round, and those that have grooves.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you understand the symptoms to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if it doesn't hurt you, then put vinegar in the wound and keep it there for an hour until the skin becomes numb;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work, as long as the stone is hard, and have at hand the instruments I told you about in removing stones for home use to help you with your task;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if you can't do it without it hurting him, and the artery has been cut off, then apply the powder on the wound and hold it tightly with bandages and don't try again. Leave the stone alone and don't remove it by force, lest perhaps the patient dies;
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has calmed and the wounds are healed, return to your work while the stone remains intact.
de hernie carnouse	of fatty hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Gelatinous moisture is nothing else but a gathering of moisture or white grease, which resides in the belly of cows, that contains the egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And it is called "grease," and there is no clean egg fabric within the shell if one believes that this is another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And this is the skin around the scrotum between the white testicles that we have described;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And it does not contain any small opening.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of these blisters is due to weakness that affects the kidneys, and spreads this substance.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And never let there be a percussion on the testicles, and this moisture takes many forms:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it becomes yellow like jaundice, or without redness, or black, or watery white, and this happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this condition; for if it is white like we have described, then it indicates an abscess formation, and extends as long as the shape of an egg, and does not affect the testicles, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the proper membrane, then it indicates an abscess with part of the egg, and because of this, we think it's another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	And if moisture is between the skin of the joints and the white bone, you will feel it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	Therefore, when you know the color of the moisture, if you test all around the involved area, from which its shape is as described.

de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the spleen

dou chastrement	of chastity

et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the lump:

de percier lou fondement	To pierce the foundation

de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula from its foundation

si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And always make the abscesses in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and when you puncture the abscess from within, and it's located under the skin above the foundation, take a tool to pierce through the head according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I bend one thread into an 'S', and place the needle with all of the thread in the abscess until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perfectly within the margin beneath the foundation inside, then extract the thread of that broken one, as if you bend your hand or base.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and join the two parts together, and bind one to the other, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it back each time, until the threads come through these barriers that are between two, and connect;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed and sanitized.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not perforate, make it pierce in every way you can, provided it's not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For one should not make the incision too deep through the puncture stitch, and then treat it as we have said, while it remains clean.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spike-shaped sputum that one makes into a fistula is rather thick and from one side and trenching;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand not, because with that one should neither make nor avoid making it as you see here:
des emorroydes	From hemorrhages
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Fatigues are according to two ways:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	They can be found within the foundation like small and large pieces of resin. If there are many or just one such piece, they adhere to the foundation and penetrate it from beneath and up to the main part of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that lie outside require very little moisture, and even if they adhere or a bit of lemon water or just a bit of blood, and have the color of brown;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those inside the foundation, you must instruct the patient to expel them through the air in chambers, until the foundations release, and they notice the threads;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, place them in tweezers or hold them with your fingernail, then remove them from their roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if they cannot hold them by their moisture, then take them in the handkerchief, or on cotton, or from a piece of camlet;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And remove them with your fingers, then cover them and dust them with some hot powders that are for the fire cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you burn them as it is said or according to the chapter on cautery, and treat them with other remedies until they heal;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the fundament cannot come out, then treat the patient with astringent and harsh remedies for colic to help wash what is inside or at the fundament, so that it can come out smoothly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient does not improve and if their strength is weak for the fundament, then the treatment should be gentle;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you should hold them at your nail or with tongs, and grasp them, then cut them in accordance with what we have said, as long as the blood flows, and as long as they fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you sew according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread and make it into a needle. Then pass the thread through and pierce the needle from the other side, and loop two ends of the thread around the needle. And let them be wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	Tighten the thread in a neat form, then tie the thread, and remove the needle. Do this for all others, and leave some to manage excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the wound a moistened cloth in oil or a poultice, and place it on the wound. Instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then let it grow until it is complete, and when they have fallen, if you apply ointment treatment and other treatments, until it heals properly.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	do drying by sweat or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times it causes bowel dryness within the intestines, and due to natural constraints, and when the illness is old and medicine no longer works.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary for you to place the tip of a needle or on your nail the skin above, which should not be left moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then treat it until it heals properly as is fitting;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, redo the shaving more vigorously than before, until it heals completely, and is scraped clean;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it has fully healed.
dou fremit	with trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Formications are small irregularities on the skin before a boil forms, and they go deep into the flesh;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And once the vein is constricted, and it feels like shaking from cold, and this sensation can be felt all over the body, especially more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a stalk from a goose feather or a strong hawk feather and place this stick over the twitching area, until the purplish circles cover the entire twitching.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all the stick until you cover the entire twitching area and place it evenly, and eradicate the twitching from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see this, do as follows with a spider's hair or iron according to this shape, and let it be slender underneath and sharp above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Don't pierce it, as you must hold with both hands, and gently press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see the twitching, apply heat to it, in accordance with where or before the section of the cautery method is described.
de la forme dou clistere	Of the shape of the bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	None of the time make an abscess of silver or lead, or melted spider;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And never use these small and large instruments according to where they should be applied.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those thus take on the task of healing children and those who are weak and painful, being little.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the bladder is small at the top and large, or the belly is bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And there is a need where the belly might be tied, as you see, and the child pierced within.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And has on one side two missing parts, and on the other one;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let's put medicines on the belly like from a beast bladder or parchment. It should be pierced all around by small missing parts, and there should be one inch of space between each part. Then insert into these parts threads about an inch long that have been twisted together in a crimped manner, either X times or 9 times around, and sew the belly shut like you would sew a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie it with a strong thread in front of the instrument, then proceed to cauterize;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And this forms a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and smear the head with oil from a thorn bush or an egg yolk, or something similar, then gently apply it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then have the doctors hold their two hands together on it while it is still fully visible, then remove the lump, and gently lift the patient's legs onto the surface, and if the medicine seems to be coming out, extract as much as you can.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if it sleeps through one whole night, that is more effective help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you use it to treat illness characterized by the loosening of abdominal contents, and the medicine seeks to quickly emerge, then continue using it as long as it is effective.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if it's bleeding from the vein or from an abscess, then let the lump be as subtle as for a baby;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the shape of the subtle lump under whose skin tension exists:
des plaies	from wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have spoken about the treatment of wounds in the section on wound care;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will tell you about hand treatments and medicines, according to their application.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and where on the body they occur, and why they have occurred.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that cause wounds are by the impact of a stone, and the cut from a sword or knife, or from a spear or staff or axe, or similar actions;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or when they are caused by the actions of the body, such as a wound on the neck, or head, or chest, or belly, or liver, and similar parts;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you how to treat each wound, and start with head wounds, since the recollection will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and there is no break in the bone, be careful if it's by stone or similar actions, and even if all the skin has been torn open and the wound is large, you might slightly suspect an abscess.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	If it results in quick healing of the head part itself, even if there is slight bleeding from the wound, and then heal against the direction of the removed part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And let the patient consume their bodily fluids replenished with wine and fatty meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if they do not wish to heal quickly, let them reduce their meat intake, and refrain from drinking wine or eating red meats;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place in the wound, if an abscess forms and breaks open, use moistened cotton in oil rose or only in rosmary-infused wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no pus, apply to the wound, if it has fresh blood and isn't disturbed by air, powder, which I will describe later;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if his strength has been drained, then apply some remedies until he is restored.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a tailor and similar, and the lips cannot be joined together by stitches, then join them with suturing, as I would say for wounds in the belly, from the suture.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound exposes bone, and pain, but only for a little while, if you can.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh instead of skin. Instruct the patient to eat hearty meats such as roasted testicles, wheat, and other similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or skin is putrefying, and it doesn't reach to the bone, then cut out all of the rotting flesh, and cleanse.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is blood in the wound or vein without clotting, and it cannot be stemmed with medicine, then stop up the artery. If you find an exposed one, tie it with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not benefit, then apply cautery.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if the wounds are small and simple, then they require light treatment:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and if you mix this powder which binds together like that once the iron has passed through.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And the way of making this powder is:
pren encens une partie;	take some frankincense;
sanc de dragon II parties;	add two parts of dragon's blood;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	add three parts of fresh garlic, grind it finely, apply to the wound, and bind it firmly until it airs well and adheres to all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	then mix well, leave it without bandaging if it does not swell;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	For one does not remove the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And this must be done with a salve alone, not with incense or the blood of dragons, but when the medicine has healed the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the heart has made the wound bleed, even when it is in this state, I do not say that one should apply this powder.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some medicated poultices, or oat flour mixed with water and honey, until the bleeding stops;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue other treatments until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if bone breakage occurs with the wound and it's small, then use delicate tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about bone fractures later.
de la plaie dou col	from the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This wound originates near the neck and is straightforward, if there's no distinction between it and beneath the chin, but if something within the neck or artery has been cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the neck, without any other concern than leaving the treatment alone and not putting anything that might restrict it, because it harms the neck and makes them pull away;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not put anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and the continuity of such things is with the brain, which is the highest member.

de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	From the wound of a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it's from a spear or knife and the wound is deep, observe if there is wind escaping from the wound; if the patient is bleeding, act accordingly:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	So you know that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And if it is not deep, and it retains all its blood, if one does not apply the powder immediately in the first hour, or bind it with no risk of the blood escaping completely, and returns to the heart, causing the body to weaken, then care for the afflicted person;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	but apply an attractive balm, and bind it twice a day;

et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good conditions, know that the wound is saved.

et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	and if it cannot heal or work normally, know that there may be an opening.
si la cure si com on doit.	if the treatment is as it should be.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it is simple, or worse, or on the back, then treat as the one in front instructs;
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	and if it's large, stitched;
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	and if it's small, powdered, and if it's deep into the bone, or has splinters, clean out the wound and remove any external treatments if they are exposed;
