dou derrompement dou ventre	From the rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The belly distensions are large, medium, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound, one might have an ejection of the intestines, or parts of the intestines, through which foreign objects can enter;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the stitching is more complicated; for once, it's worse than small injuries compared to large ones, because in stitching up the intestines repeatedly over time, one would not risk sewing them back together if they were not stitched step by step.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell even when they feel cold; if one sews them too tightly again, it's better to make small injuries. Therefore, one should gently stitch the intestines back to their original position rather than attempting to repair larger ones.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And know that the rupture of the belly occurs according to four ways:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common stitches occur at the belly wound, and the stitch of other chest injuries are associated with other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Yet they are more precise with the stitch of the belly, and I will say each one and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small and nothing of the intestine has been torn out, and if there's something to be sewn back together, this can be done through one of the two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	Or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	Moisten an sponge or add the salt in water only, or you cook in boiling water with ginger and cypress and thorns, and remove the intestines until the blood is drained;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this wine has been reduced, and made thick so it can help in reducing swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the blood departing, rinse the intestines with water or wine until they are cooked well, because through this, the entrance allows passage of little things;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, then slightly widen the wound with the instrument used to remove blood clots;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	And the first treatment should be made thick so that there is no unnecessary cutting of the size, because I don't have it;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And these are the tools to split them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut from within in the bend and not outward, and see this form:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines escape, if you can set them back according to their natural shape in their own proper place, because this is what matters, for it counts.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide, and it's in the lower part of the abdomen, then it is necessary to have the patient lie on their back, and put their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	And if it's in the lower part of the abdomen, then put the head and bottom higher than the lower parts, and similarly if the belly wound is in one of the two halves, place yourself so that the injured half is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus it is necessary to follow what I say for large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds use what is suitable to you, then have at your disposal the entire surgical kit that sears the entire wound with its hand and joins the edges;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	And this is the common method of suturing, and you take one or more needles according to the size of the wound's width. Then leave about half an inch at the edge of the wound, then you place a needle where there will be enough strong thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	and pierce the two ends of the skin with the two ends of the stitch, which is inside the skin, as long as you make it pierce that part, and join the two ends of the stitch together in four.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	then take two strands of thread and tie them together on the needle from both sides. Then join the two ends of the wound together slightly overlapping them, and then leave about half an inch, then place another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	then tie the thread in the same way you did with the first needle, and continue doing this according to your skill with needles until all the wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	And use needles that are midway in size, between fine and thick ones, for the fine needles cut all the flesh, and the overly thick cannot enter well at all.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because it is necessary that they be midway;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and it is not good to have the needles too far out of the flesh and skin, for they would cut and widen the wound before sewing.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and when you stitch the wounds with needles, ensure they don't irritate the patient while sleeping, and cover the needle holes with cloths or bandages to keep them clean until the wound heals.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	And this way of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds, because one or two needles are sufficient.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second stitch is common, and it involves assembling two bones from the skin and two bones from the muscle together on one needle or thread where there is one strong thread midway;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	And when you have pierced all four bones together, you should reset the needle at the part where you started, in the manner one sews clothes;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place an interval between each stitch as large as a half of a small coin.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	These stitches sew up the wound, and I stitched a belly that had been cut by a sword, which was torn open, resulting in a wound longer than one hand-width, and contained two hand-widths of intestines, and the wound was in the middle of the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I brought back the intestine until it had been out for twenty-four hours, and the wound healed up to fifteen days, and I treated him, and he recovered.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they thought that he was dying, it was indeed a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And I would not cure it with ointment, because there was none to be found where I was or any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	I will wipe the wound with old cloth twice a day, and wash it in honey water until it was clean.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper methods of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and pierce from the outer part up to that inner side;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	When it has pierced the center straight up and down, place the tip of the needle at the siphon or wound or where you have punctured with the needle, and make it pierce from the inner side to this outer part;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And the understanding of this stitching is that you sew in the same way as the marten furs leather, and you leave once on one side of the siphon, and take it again from another, until the stitching is fully completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of stitching, that Galen accurately described, is such that nobody does it. They instead unite the two parts naturally together and apply one end of the thread to the other in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	Stake an awl or stick near the elbow area and make just one hole in that part only, leaving two ends of the needle;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	Then twist the awl, and make it pierce from the outer part right through to here inside, until both ends of the needle.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both from the outer part right through to here inside using two other awls that are opposite to each other;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the way of stitching and it is the most common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	Galen said this sentence, and nobody denies it; one must stitch the belly with two needles, or where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and must one stick one needle on the side and the other on the opposite side, like those who sew inlays;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	and know that when the wound is inside the belly, the stitching is more painful than in their other wounds.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The assessment of the injury is like that of the assessments of other injuries:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and so that when you find the fresh injury full of blood, just like how heat has treated it, you should return to its natural state, and then stitch;
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	then put on the stimulating powder for charcoal, and if heat has treated it, then apply no lotion that is available until the injury heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And heat the needle, and let them sew up the cut, and mend the wound;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as usual until it is clean;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And if you don't have remedies, place them, alternately, until it starts to bleed, old cotton, and stir it twice a day until it is clean.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	But you need no other remedy in multiple forms when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	And if you doubt that the wound might affect major limbs, it is necessary for you to immerse light wool in oil with a moderate heat or in rose oil, and place it inside the joints, and cover the surrounding areas;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	And if there is pain or gangrene in the bowels, and it happens repeatedly, then give them a black wine enema, and similarly if gangrene has reached up to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And makes a puncture inside, and you know that when it is large intestine, it is easier to heal than the smaller ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestine that is called 'the young' cannot heal when it's injured, and this is due to the position of the veins involved, and because of the subtlety of the entire body, and the approach of its nature towards nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if pus jumps from the wound, if it resets behind as with an intestine while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	And if it is old and has turned to blood or blackness, you should tie the area that is black, so no bleeding occurs from there, for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	Then cut the one that is between the tie, and place the two heads hanging from the part under the wound until past it for easing extraction when pus quits, and the wound closes.
de la routure dou boueil	from the rupture of the bladder
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestine is firm, and the wound is small, you can restore it in some ways, because I have seen that a brave man's belly was pierced by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And there was a wound on the right side of the stomach, and it became inflamed and developed into a fistula, causing malabsorption and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I performed the cure according to my abilities and did not stop refining until it was healed, and bound his limbs.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw him healing, I wondered if the patient might be experiencing pain in their abdomen;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And there was no illness, but he improved and ate and drank;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And it is said by some experts that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be treated in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	Take large intestines, then join the edges of the wound. When the intestines open their mouths, place them on the two edges if they pull their mouth upwards;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	And then one grips the head, and it is held in such a way that it cannot be released, after which another movement occurs in this manner right after the first, as before, until the entire wound has healed.
et cout la plaie.	and there is the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	That is the chief that gets into the intestines, and it causes no harm to the patient, and one can bind the intestine with a fine thread that has been cut from an animal's intestine in such a manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Take the end of this intestine thread that is most charred, and then tie it to the end of the other thread made from fine linen. Twist both threads together, sew them onto a needle, and stitch the intestine, then reset it in its place;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	This method of sewing is solely done according to the path of engagement and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it's in one of the intestines, if there's no injury or illness, because of its subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from a fistula or wherever it may be.
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	Know that every wound or abscess, as it matures, is universally termed 'fistula', and even when hairy and round in shape.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And a fistula is according to the firm and white congealing, where no pain is felt, and it's also covered like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes it appears clearly white, and at other times it's thickened;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes it's small, and at other times it's quite significant;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	And I have spoken about this in the section on wounds, that any wound that is not healed and contains no pus, leaves only through one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	This means, by the weakness of blood or pus;
ou por sa malice;	because of its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within, and on the lips, that does not allow new growth;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or it has too much blood;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the ears are infected, and the substance is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine used in treatment is not good;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because of the way it spreads like a plague;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or due to its late properties in that region, digestion is delayed and health also lags, fleeing naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or it has veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicine in this section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	So it is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of fistulas which is done by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistula occurs in all limbs of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	because there are fistulas that come from the large veins, and arteries, and nerves, or in the thorax, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs, or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the property of the main member, and exhibits the symptoms accordingly.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that occur in this manner are difficult to heal, and there is no exception but labor and lack of knowledge;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And if there is no fistula that does not reach until what I have said, and you take the care of the cure, and you know how to recognize it; then use a spider web or iron wire tent, if the fistula is straight, then insert it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	And if the fistula is twisted, try to find a subtle path of penetration, for the needles bend and move along the twists;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	And if the fistula has lost its ends and you cannot properly seek it through attempts, try enemas through one of the ends, for moisture flows from one end to another, and cleanses;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	Then carefully inquire with your strength, to know if there is bone or nerve, and if it feels like hair underneath. Ask the patient about the pain they feel when you press on it, and where exactly that pain is;
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	And when you truly know the location of it and that it is far from joints, nerves, arteries or veins, or any other places I've mentioned, proceed according to what I've said; remove bone fragments and clear away putrid substances that are inside.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	And then the treatment until it is healed, and if a sinus has formed, deeply dig in the correct location. It's necessary that you carve out as much as possible. Then place wet cloths with medical ointment, and let them soak up to the tip of the sinus. Continue until the medicine has eroded away any excess substance remaining at the bottom.
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then place clean dressings, until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if it has not healed by this method, then cauterize as we have instructed, and if the bone is decayed from the sinus, then remove it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	And if the vein or major limbs are obstructed or hindered in any way, as we have said.
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if the bone is exposed, and there is decay and darkness, then remove it until all decay is removed. Then dress with clean substances until it heals;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	And if there is no healing, and the bone returns as before, know that you have not yet reached your goal.
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	If it discovers and desires until you reach the bottom, and removes all the corruption, then return the bone;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is already healed, that is well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption has gone too far, that you cannot bring it back;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other reason than to abandon it by nature;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles, si l’estrai a I estrument covenauble a ceu, et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there is only a small corrupted bone, and you can pull it with tweezers, take it using the appropriate instrument for that. If there are many bones, remove them all, do not leave any of them;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour, si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	And if moisture opposes this against it, with no error or fear, handle moisture, heat, and flesh, and liberate the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture, et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os, et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And if you cannot extract them within an hour, put something to stanch the wound on it for gangrene, and leave it as long as the flesh is gangrened inside the bones, and then they will remove the bones more easily;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse, si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee, puis restoure la plaie;	And if it's a large bone, such as in the leg or thigh, just remove the putrefaction until all of the bone turns black, then close the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is a large portion of decayed flesh and it has reached down to the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	And if it suits to treat everything up until the decay, and then treat it until it heals completely;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint I home en sa jambe, si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	And I will tell you of a case where a fistula occurred in someone's leg, so that you may take it as an example and seek help for your own work.
Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	He was a young person around thirty years old, who experienced pain in his leg due to an issue inside the body that caused substances to travel down to the leg, leading to a large abscess forming, and there seemed to be no reason for it to open.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri, et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	However, through their foolishness they opened it as wide as the abscess allowed, and within, they ate away at a great amount of substances, and became a fistula, and he suffered much loss that all groaned over and was affected by body moisture;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor II ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains, tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit, et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And many doctors treated him for over two years, and there was no wise person in the art of healing hands until I was called, and when I saw his leg and the remedies being used to cure him, and that which ate away through the losses by great bodily suffering;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And became red the body of youth, and had a yellowish hue.

I pitched a tent in one of these depressions, and then searched all the depressions, finding that some came against each other from all parts of the leg.

je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I was the part that appeared from the decayed bone, and I thought there was no other decay, as it was only what I had exposed;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And began to treat the wound with medicines over time, and couldn't heal it;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant, et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	And then I began again, and found the bone in the same manner as before, and found the decay continuing within the bone, and it too was affected, and I removed it, and tried to heal the wound;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole, puis le restourai de medicines;	But I could not do much until I copied about one hand of bone length, and treated it with all its parts, then returned it using medicine;
et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment, et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir, et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	And it healed and fused quickly, and no longer required resuming the operation except for the weakness of the patient who couldn't endure it, and because of my fear of his death.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement, et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	For blood evacuation often occurs, but it was completely healed. In its place of the bone, a hard flesh formed, and it had good disposition and didn't cause any harm or opposite effect at all from beginning to end, neither inside nor outside.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it should be treated in this manner:
pren I liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert, et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	Take hold of it, and pull at the part of the bone that is exposed, and instruct them to extend it upwards;
et met I autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os, et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz, et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and place another thread of thicker wool than the first one, and bind it over the flesh that is inside the bone, and pull the contaminated flesh upwards, revealing the flesh on the part you want to heal, making sure not to hurt the flesh;
et met I tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And place a charcoal or a board under the bone to draw out the putrid flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	And it is necessary to remove as much as one can see and feel the corruption, and also remove again later if needed.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie, si descuevre la char toute;	And if the bone is corrupted and does not open, and corruption is in the middle or a part, then remove all of the flesh;

si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	If you consider the tool that you need according to what it requires.
dou feu	by fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The joints might dislocate due to an internal cause, or due to an external one;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie, si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient, si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	And when you have treated that erosion by the cure of medicines, and if they do not benefit, it is necessary to amputate that limb up to where the erosion occurs, so that the patient escapes through death or through malice, which is greater than the fault of the limb;

si te haste dou coper, et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans, se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main. et je te conterai k’il avint a I home en som piet:	And I will tell you what happened at my house one evening:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu, et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	It happened to him one night that it seemed like a darkness as if of fire, and this corruption came first to his foot at the heel, until it encompassed the entire foot;

de l’aposteme de l’ungle	Of the abscess under the nail.
