et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And while being on top of the board under the stomach of the patient, make sure it is well aligned.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And you must not forget the other things that I have said about other breaks, once we have discussed them;
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	And assist with each injury as it is necessary.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	Regarding the breaking of the bone in the hand.
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bone of nature in the woman is broken, if she is made to stay swollen, then she is laid on the lower part of the back, and held from behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the cavity that is natural to the patient with cotton, and put in similarly large amounts as needed;
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then stand the woman up, and raise her back gradually, and then jump out the cotton until it reaches the entry of natural anatomy, and return the bone with this action;
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she wishes to urinate, remove the cotton, and once she has urinated, let her return to it, and thus do this for seven days or more.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If the break will be restored, and if you see fit, take a goat bladder, and fasten it at one end with a reed, and let the entire bladder fill into natural anatomy;
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then breathe into the straw form, until the bladder is inflated inside:
la nature si revenra li brisure;	Nature will cause the break to heal;
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then fill it with cotton, and let it remain for some days, until it is sound.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the bone of the hand or foot of a man is broken, or of a woman, if you restore it as we have said for the thigh bone;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	And do not ignore these neighboring breaks that he who puts his study and use to it should attend to, and listen to my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the break signifies many different positions for the correct way of restoration:
enten le donques.	Understand it therefore.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the testicles, when they are broken, take a goose's neck and insert it into the testicle;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	Then wrap it with lint, and leave it for three days or until healed from the inside, and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	By fracture with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for the one who has a fracture with a wound, even if it's large, like in the case of the thigh bone or shoulder blade or similar, that they be surgically treated now, so that the surgeries we have mentioned testify to this.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound is clean, then seal it with vitriol, or if you have nothing else, then start to treat the fracture at that same hour, or on that day, assuming no abscesses appear.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if abscesses appear, then let the treatment continue until a new day, as long as the abscess is calming down, and don't touch it on the third or fourth day, for you would cause harmful accidents.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the bone is broken and visible at its exposed knee, then it should be put back together lightly with your hands, in a small extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if it extends beyond what you can equip with your hands, take this iron instrument which has seven or eight inches in length, and the width is according to the size of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	And for this, the surgeon must apply three or four times, according to how many times he needs it in each case of injury;
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	And make it round and slightly thick so that it doesn't bend under pressure on the limb inside your body, and make it pointed at both ends, and large in the middle forward, like this:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called "palainche" for this reason, so that the curved shoulder should be placed on the head of the visible bone;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	And when it is put back once, as long as it regrows, and so that one is equal to the other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the break is subtle and the tools cannot properly grasp the bone, it requires that you place the tip of the bone until the tools have capability.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot return the bone back, as we have said, if you have access to an appropriate tool for this, such as a saw or file, by your power;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	Then remove the one that is stuck in the bone due to its hardness and small flakes.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is returned, and the patient feels intense pain afterwards, know that it has not been placed in its natural position.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Do so until it is in its place, then wet the bandage in black medicinal wine, and properly if it is internal;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not put tallow or any other thing that might smell on the wound, which could lead to gangrene and decay;
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	Then administer these [treatments] when you have restored the bone, and leave the wound exposed, and cover it entirely, according to the size of the wound, and be sure to ensure that the wound is not constrained with bruising.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	And many times this has happened to the fool, and it brought either death or corrosion upon the patient every time;
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and let the compresses be softer and more soothing than other injuries.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is bad or large, and you doubt that harmful accidents have occurred there, as we have said, and you find pain in the limb, then it should not be placed under these [treatments];
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	but wrap entirely around the limb instead of these compresses, with hard cloths and tie them in place.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see that after one or two days the wound is swelling, remove whatever you have put on it with vinegar, and apply healing ointment for wounds, such as the fourfold medicine and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And it must be that you dislocate the limb twice a day, morning and evening, until it is joined and sound.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it should have been so that the limb is bound in such a way that the bone slides down slightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if it continues for the whole day, and it cannot join anymore, know that there are small fragments of bone, so you must seek to open the wound with a probe, and remove all these necessary pieces that cause pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a sinus develops in the hand or any other form of corruption, it is necessary to treat it according to what was instructed in the chapter before this one.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken, and an opening made in the body, such as the bones of the shin or shoulder, or other parts of the large limbs, do not attempt to set them immediately because many times this leads to death, but leave it until they heal;
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	By chance, wait for up to 20 or 30 days, then treat the wound if possible;
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	And if you cannot, leave it as it is.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	The burns that come from sweat
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	Many times after the healing of the breakage, especially if it's near the joint, there's something to observe regarding the shape of the limb;
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	And by chance, the limbs cannot perform their natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Therefore, take care if it seems that there is fluid:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If they administer stiff medicines such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, as well as sarcocolle, caragana, and similar others, do so by taking any of these things individually or all together, and mix them with stoptive wine or in abundance of an egg or with oil;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and apply them on the wound as wafers, and hold them well in place, and don't remove them with your hands during the day;
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	and then reset it again, repeating until all dislocations have been removed;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you hold onto a well-made piece of plaster.
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	for the property of plaster is such that it extracts all swellings from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the dislocation has turned into hardness like bone and needs extraction, if it has formed a lump underneath, and remove any excess that is visible.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If you are handling it on any bone, as long as it is intact, and during treatment until it heals.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	Of the limb that becomes weak after an illness.
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the fracture of the bone has been restored and remains after the limbs are weak and fine, this happens due to various reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	It's because when it was tied too tight and wasn't tied as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	Or perhaps because there were too many ligatures, and the body couldn't come into its own in the limb;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to excess bleeding;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or because of too large movements, not in their time;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	Or perhaps because there is little blood in his body, it becomes weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment involves you feeding the patient, making them weak, until the sickness has multiplied within them;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and administer baths, and give them joy and laughter;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then apply wax to the limb, so that the wax attracts towards the large artery, and often rinse it with tepid water, until the swelling aligns with the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and restores his natural appearance.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	The member becomes twisted after recovery.
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limbs are twisted after restoration, and if bones were broken openly, even though the shape of the limb is deformed, still it does not lose its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	do not believe the fools who say one must break the limb anew entirely, and many people have done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	And these actions are criticized, and they lead to great harms, and by chance one dies;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	Still, if nodations and torture are involved, they should be treated with hot water, or if soothing herbs are cooked, such as the leaves of the angelica plant, roots, and meadowsweet, among similar things;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	And you should apply a soothing ointment, such as properly prepared tallow, and take angelica oil, and mix it with lard or the oil of sesame, then apply it topically;
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	Or you take dried figs and grind them with cow dung, and similar remedies that reduce inflammation.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And no time is removed the operation of rubbing continuously and for a long time with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And let each body part move once an hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the stiffness has hardened and become as firm as bone, such as in bones, and requires being treated with hot iron, if it's necessary to operate up until the bone, making incisions gently and delicately;
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	And apply concentration and study to the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This begins the book on dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing great pain and injury to the patient.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation affects none, if now is needed bring back without hesitation.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if one delays, they swell up, and by chance, when one tries to reset them at the joint;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	By heaven, it is not right for one to move them at that time when they are swollen:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	Often brings on nausea and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	However, when this happens, if you find the patient is ill, then leave them alone until all abscesses are relieved;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then immerse the limb in hot water and oil, then reset it gently, and treat each limb according to how the treatment should occur at its joint.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have organized the chapters about shoulder dislocations up to this point.
des mandibules	of the jaws
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	Sometimes the jaws are dislocated backward, and dislocations of both occur in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	These are somewhat hardened at their ends, and slightly softened;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	They are completely dislocated, hanging towards the anus, and they let saliva from their mouth which they cannot contain or close their mouth, and wrap their tongue with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it can often return through several positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is whole and complete, you must reset it quickly, without delay;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a way that the ministers cut into the chief of the bad side, and thrust the sights from his pocket with one hand into the root of the dislocation of the jaw within the mouth, if the dislocation is two parts;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other should be done with both hands to make it even;
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	And instruct the patient to soften them, his jaws, and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And guide her until she settles back into its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it is difficult to return them, especially when they are the two jaws combined, so that their heads are immersed in hot water and oil, until lightly resetting them;
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Nor be troubled to set them again, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are returned equally, and the mouth of the patient is closed properly with soothing, then place wet cloths in a poultice made from rose oil and beeswax, then bind them loosely with moist thread;
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	And let the patient rest on their back, and have their shoulders lying between two pillows, so that they do not move to either side, nor try to strain, but only consume light food, until the pains subside, and secure the jaws;
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then judge if he wants to eat lightly, and there is no work in opening the mouth for eating and drinking, until the lower jaw is well healed and cured.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be properly aligned within an hour and are not converted back to their original positions, then fevers and recurrent swelling occur, along with occasional abdominal discomfort, and occasionally, vomiting of pure fluids.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see that, then know it's destruction;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	And many times has death occurred to those it befalls, within nine days.
de la forcelle	from the lever
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The strength cannot relieve from within the middle of the back and at its base, and is dislocated outwards every time, and one feels this well indeed.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the healing is that the patient lies on their back and extends their arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	And then press the limb against your palm, and it will return to its proper shape;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	Then place on the plaster and the bandage, and keep it in place;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	And the head which is towards the blade cannot be dislocated;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	If it cannot stay in place even once, then reset it to its original position, just as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then place on the plaster and bind it tightly, then instruct the patient to rest until they are healed.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And similarly, bring back the shoulder blades when it has returned to its place after being dislocated.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Concerning the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the shoulder is only dislocated according to three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	The first way is when it dislocates from the part of the clavicle towards downward;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	And the second way is when it dislocates from the part of the base;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	And by chance dislocates from the top part, and this happens rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	And does not dislocate behind for the shoulder, and does not dislocate inside for the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	And it gets dislocated multiple times from above to below, even in those with little flesh, for these jump out quickly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	For those who have enough flesh, it jumps to the bones and returns to them.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And by chance, some men suffer from impact or fracture, and the shoulder swells due to an abscess, and they believe that it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	So you must verify it, as long as you are sure;
et adonques encomence la cure.	And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And you will recognize dislocation when it moves towards the shoulder, and you'll make a distinction between the diseased shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find a clear manifestation of their diversity;
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	And you will find a hollow at the shoulder's head, and from the elbow to the shoulder, like it's an opening;
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	And the patient cannot bring their hand to their nose, nor move it with any movements;
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	Furthermore, if it is dislocated at the top, as long as it isn't completely hidden, because you clearly find it at the socket;
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	This method of dislocation can only be resolved by repositioning, when it is new, or if the child has been injured.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is that the ministers lift the hand from the flesh at the top, then place their thumbs on the socket, and lift the joint upward forcefully to the shoulder;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	And the ministers lift the hand, then extend it upwards, before placing it on top of something.
si venra hastanment.	If it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come out as we have said within several days after, it is necessary that the patient be bathed in hot water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the attendant should apply gentle soothing treatments, such as a decoction of rue, fenugreek and borage in hot water, and it should be administered;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then sew the wound on the back of the patient, and place a pillow of evenly soft wool under their buttocks, neither too hard nor too soft. Then place the heel against the pillow, and raise the shoulder joint gently, and guide the hand towards the body of the patient;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and another attendant should keep hold on the shoulder joint from below, so that it does not move upwards;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	this shoulder should now return to its position, and if you see that the realignment is being done in this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	And indeed you must have a space at home that is larger than the person;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	And make it straight toward the chest, and place your shoulder under the edge of the person, and lift the edge up so that the body hangs down below.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	And another helper should stretch out their hand from behind the body towards the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too weak, they cannot support anything heavy with him, and the dislocation returns immediately.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And you can reset it in other ways as well:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And you place the long stake in the ground, so that the shoulder is also positioned like a pistol, and it should not be too large or too greasy;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	Then place it under the body, but so that it has straps supporting it from below, and the person should be lying long with the length of the stake.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Then extend her hand towards the other side, form it, and the joint will return to its place quickly;
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if she does not wish to return through all these things that we have said, then perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take two elbows of strong firewood and four sticks that are wide; have the head ready to be inserted from above into the opening, according to this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	then bind the head to the rod with fabric underneath, so that the rod does not injure the patient, then place it into the opening under the affected area;
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extend your arms on the rod for its entire length, bind the shoulder onto the rod, and place the arm at the head of the hand, then put the arm on one end of a large stick, allow her hands to hang downwards, and leave her body hanging from the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint has now been reset.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when she is there, in whatever way it may be, if you must put on the seat of the dislocation an equal thread, then place plastered with powder from the mill, together with incense and egg oil, all over the shoulder and around it. Then remove that which was placed upon the seat after a while, and retie the bandage on top of the plastering, and hold the hand at its neck, and keep your hands in this state for some time.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is necessary that he eat little, until the limbs become stronger, for they will heal faster;
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then eat more after about 5 or 7 days, and start moving them;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	and if it is hardened and not softened, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is out of place due to moisture that has come upon it, or for some other reason, then you must administer three cauterizations to it, as was described in the chapter on cauterizations.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this, and it releases after about 7 days, but the joint does not hold, and cannot lift his arm up, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is compressed or stretched or weakened;
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	And know that the joint will never properly return to its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation occurring towards the buttocks and breasts or behind, if it is caused by pushing and stretching of the hands, and another treatment is applied elsewhere;
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat as long as it is clean.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing there comes weakness in the limb, and delayed movements, then the patient should take frequent baths with hot water until that weakness is alleviated, and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	From the dislocation of the shoulder joint
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	It's dislocated at the elbow joint and with poking it returns;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And it's dislocated from all sides, and in front as well as behind, and the dislocation is not responded to, because one can clearly see and feel it;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And dislocates according to each figure.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the diseased skin with healthy tissue, if you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is knotted, and cannot bend the arm, nor touch its shoulder to any degree.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And it must be reset in this manner that abscesses are removed and flow away, for if they were to flow outwards instead, there would be blame for trying to reintroduce them.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	And by chance cannot be reset completely, even when it is behind;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	It's worse than other dislocations and causes more pain, and by chance death comes from it.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And this restoration occurs, when it is such that one can bring it back, that you extend his hand to your two hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And his arms are spread out, and the hands are directed towards the center of the chest in all directions, forwards and backwards, and push the joint to its place on his wrists or at the base of his palm, as long as it returns to its position.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if there is a dislocation in front, it returns when they double their hand against their own and push from the base of the palm with the knife that has been inserted.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it doesn't want to return to place, administer strong stretching;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	And if two ministers stretch the arm and keep it stretched by both hands, so that it does not move during stretching;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	Then turn the arm in all directions, then when you have wrapped a double flag long and wide around it;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	And when the eyes touch the joint with their hand, if they apply some oil to soften the joint, then press the joint firmly, until it heals;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	And when it's in place, she places it on dry plaster with a poultice of an egg, holds it steady, and lets the arm hang by the neck towards the diseased area, and leaves it for some days, then releases it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firmly in place, she releases the bandage, and leaves it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you see that the joint is not being placed well, then start the plaster and the bandage again, and leaves it like this for some days, until it's firmly set;
puis le deslie.	Then releases it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if they feel pain after the displacement of the joint is reset, and it moves again, then they should bathe in hot water and generously scrub, pressing until their discomfort subsides;
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Or you place a sheep's fat on the joint, then leave it for one day and one night, then the surgeon performs an operation, or the person enters into a bath;
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when it sweats, gently rub the joint, then put the fat back on, and then enters into a bath;
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this two or three times until it heals properly;
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see that, put on wet cow's dung mixed with butter and apply it;
si revenra a sa disposition.	If it returns to its normal state.
li dislocation de la main	the dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The hand joint is dislocated, and the return is gentle, more so than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Otherwise, it is necessary to bring it back immediately into its place while it's dislocated, so that the limb swells or there is pus discharge.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the process of bringing it back should be like this: you place the bad hand on a board and extend the helper's hand, so that when the patient puts their palm against the appearance of the joint, you hold until they recover.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Otherwise, you should check if it's correctly back in place;
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then have the patient bend and stretch their back of the hand on a board during extension and retraction.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is in the back of the hand, then have the patient place the back of their hand on the table, and you mirror their hand onto that appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If she returns now, that's quite well.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	But if not, when the pressure of plastering material relieves abscesses, and it is left without restarting.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you cannot put her back in place after some days, if the joint remains twisted;
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and it does not harm the patient for as long as the hand is immobilized, and cannot force anything at all:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	so you know that the nerve has been cut, or the artery;
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is no other way to apply force except with the cautery in this case, and by chance there is no other option.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when his hands are in place, apply the plaster we have mentioned, then strain it and leave it for five days, then release it and leave it as such.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he can't move it well and there's no crack, then apply hot water, and rub until it is clean.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	Regarding the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	No matter how many times the elbow of the hand is dislocated in each direction, no matter on the back of the palm or belly;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	So apply pressure, and hold the dislocation in your fists until it heals. Then support the head of the shoulder, and gently guide it towards the part that is separated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and leave it for two days, and then place him evenly on that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and bind it in the manner we have described, and remove the binding on that day, and allow him to move gently, and re-bind on the next day;
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this repeatedly, until it is properly aligned, and follow the same procedure if it has been dislocated in the arm pit area. Proceed in the manner you did before, until it heals;
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and do so likewise when it has been dislocated on the other side.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	of the heel, of the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the heel, or the back, or multiple heels are dislocated, if there is no treatment, because death rushes to the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the symptoms are that the discharges jump without being voluntary, and cannot be held back. Numerous times, they soften parts of any limb or both of his legs or arms.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often, the lungs divide into four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	That which divides at the back is called "gilbositez":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The treatment involves rewarding when the gilbositez has come from childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no treatment or healing at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or impacts or similar things, according to the old methods of treatments described in great words, it does not yield any significant benefit;
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	but I have abbreviated it according to my intention and formed instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I state that when the gilbositez occurs at the belly frontwards, there is no danger or harm;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also about what comes straight into two ribs, and cannot be cured outwardly but only that which belongs specifically to the back, as I say;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And when the patient's health extends up to his face on one side equally, and has tension over him, so it does not bruise;
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then place one ember at the head in the ground and make another on top, and tie a string under the buttocks with respect to the disease near the skin, and make another at the hips, and at the knees, and at the ankles;
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	And two assistants know how to handle the strings, one at the head and the others on top, among the two embers;
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	And be well closed, the ember as we have said, and the patient places her palms on the top of the formed ember until she regains consciousness.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it doesn't return through this cure, take a board of three lengths long and place it vertically on the skin surface. If the illness is at the side, place the head of the board vertically over the affected area, then put the center of the board above the spine;
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and place his feet on the other side of the board, and press firmly until he returns to its original location;
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	And if you see that it happens at the elbow which turns towards the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And if you place two torches at the head of the sick person's arm, one hand's length apart, and in between each torch, directly underneath and above them, a palm's width of space that is half a hand.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	And place one piece of charcoal in each torch, where the elbow bends, and ensure that the torches are firmly buried in the earth, so they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And between each two sticks there is one stick turning, since they turn when you connect them, and in the two turns there are two small sticks of the length of a palm, to turn the hinge;
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	And then join the link that is among the screws towards the hinge near the head, and the other link towards the feet at the other hinge. Each of the assistants turns their hinge throughout the entire link, and the masters place the spine evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, place a desiccating plaster with plenty of egg on it, then the hot rods, and then an emetic tablet that is three inches long. This cleanses the area around the boil and the healthy portion of the spine, then tie it with a string as we have said, letting the patient experience subtle hunger until they are sane.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	And if no improvement comes at the end of health, it is necessary to administer softening and moistening medicines, together with the elixir that we have mentioned before.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	And whenever you administer an oak piece, and each time there appears the appearance in the lower spine of the back, and be careful that it is a dislocation;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	And it's the bone that opens, so we must not have any presumption:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	By chance it would bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	On the dislocations of the hip
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that the hips and shoulder joints only come from dislocations, not like other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	And the hip joint is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	From top to bottom, and from front to back;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	And more from top to bottom, and somewhat less in front to back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation from within is that when you join the diseased leg with the healthy one, it's longer, and the diseased knee opens more than the healthy one, and the diseased knee cannot bend like the healthy one would.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And it's where the limbs are swollen due to pus accumulation because the shoulder joint is coming into contact with it.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him who comes to death is that this event is contrary to what precedes.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs for someone who has been injured in front are that their leg is properly aligned according to completion;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	However, it does not bend the knee without pain, and if one tries to make it do so, it cannot before, and retains its urine, and swells the ankle, and when it walks, it goes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who goes behind, are that he cannot spread his knee, nor double it, and this leg is more twisted than the other one, and his ankle is softened, and the shoulder joint comes out under the ribs at the top of the back.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The restoration of this semblance of dislocation involves that you recognize if the dislocation is old, and it remains according to its position, so there is no treatment;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and it should not be assumed about it.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And for those where the dislocation is fresh, and there are four ways of dislocation, you should quickly return the joint, stretching it inside and outside, moving it to the right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	By chance if it returns, there is no need for further treatment.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it doesn't return in this manner, you should apply strong force and press the leg strongly with both hands, or to one place bound above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	And another attendant extends his hand over it in such a way that he pushes his hands under the axilla, then forces him with a single effort up to his waist.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and another person holds the other end of the string;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And they extend upwards and downwards all at once, until the patient rises from the ground in one go, and stays hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This stretching method applies to four similar situations; and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is correct.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If this doesn't happen, then treatment should be given according to its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the shoulder joint, it's necessary to have the patient lying on their healthy side, then place the string under the root of the axilla. Afterwards, raise the leg which is out of the socket, and pull the string upwards towards the socket, using force;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then ask for other helpers to hold his arms, and encircle the large part of the elbow muscle, and extend it towards the back in line.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	If it returns to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	And this method of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you can't squeeze it in this way as we have said, then you should bind the two legs of the patient together with a strong and solid rope above both ankles and both knees, and make sure that the diseased leg is extended more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	Then have it hung from the top of a post, and allow for two long lengths of land above it;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then command the helper to encircle the elbow joint, and have other helpers accompany with the patient, who should encircle the elbow in its form. For now, the joint returns quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is at the front, if the patient lies down, as we have said in the case of someone with arthritis, and pulls on the leg's tendon directly over the painful area and also on the chest.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two pokers, one on the head and the other at the ankle, then insert the poker between the buttocks of the patient in a position near the painful area;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And wet the bandages, to prevent burning of the patient, then have each practitioner stretched out towards him, and place the shoulder's position evenly with his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it comes back, that's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it doesn't return to its place, put it on a surface like a table and press it in this manner as we described with glibosity, having the patient lie there, and have them rest on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it must involve stretching the painful leg quickly, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And place the shoulder in its painful position on the outer side of the leg, then press with the other hand, and stretch it downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is at the front, it does not suit to extend the patient's back, nor lift them up from the ground. Instead, they should be in a position as if their hip was dislocated at the front like we have said about lying between two hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	And place them on their face, and have the neck stretched out as we said before, and one should apply pressure to the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	And it will be correct when the patient extends their legs and they become equal in length.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then adjust the thighs, place the plaster, and tie with a bandage so that the hip doesn't move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And let them rest for three or four days, then release them and place the plaster again.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see they are even, pull them as before, and let them rest for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then reset it, and let it be well-stabilized, until the limb is properly set.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the hip
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knees are dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	This means, inside and outside, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	And do not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at their knee. If they cannot straighten it to its full length, this indicates that the dislocation has occurred;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all this is that you make the patient lie straight, extend their leg if they can, and place them on their back with their feet on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take his thigh bone between your palms, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the thigh bone that form;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and also other attendants extend his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the signs are that he properly aligns his leg with his thigh lightly;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and place the plaster, and let the leg rest on the thigh, and join them tightly for three or four days, then release it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not let the muscles contract until the limbs are strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limbs are not at all, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, as long as it is sane.
de la dislocation dou talon	From the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes partially dislocated and sometimes fully out, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	The signs that occur are when the ankle swells and tries to move forward at the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reinsertion should be gentle, and when it has been correctly placed alone by the person, one must gently extend it with their hands.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is relieved completely, then it must be made to stand the ill person straight, and hold them up by their right leg from above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then pull the leg towards you with your right hand, and then also to the left twice, then lift them up high, and firmly hold the leg high.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, pulling and moving the leg;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it comes back, that's good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, start the procedure again because it will come back.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return in this way, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and bury the rod firmly into the earth between their buttocks, and tie the cloth tightly around them so that they do not hurt the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then the ministers cut the fat, and some other ministers stretch out his legs at his hands or around his neck, so they tie them up on the neck of the animal.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then each minister equally extends them, and the animal should be placed between the animal's legs so as to hold the patient when they are extended.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then place the dislocated joints at his hands, and some other ministers cut the healthy leg at the knee, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is at the right point, put on the plaster and bandage it up, then tighten properly, and tie the leg to the other leg, and guard the nerves that are under the ankle from behind, so that the ligaments do not become too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the wound heals properly, then strain it.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then release it on the third day or quarter, and instruct the patient to walk for three days afterwards;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if it progresses until this point, it's not safe to assume that it won't dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when abscesses begin to drain, you should soothe them as we have said in other parts of the text, while they are still clean.
des dois	Of the cautery tool directed by fire, command the patient to let their hairs grow long and uniform; and if they start pricking at their base, keep the eyes steady so they don't move until they fully grow.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulders are dislocated, if they should be nicely extended for work, it is a simple task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in neither the neck nor the foot, it's necessary to have the patient sit on his full height or halfway sitting down, and place your foot where the joints are open. Press firmly with your foot until they heal;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when it's even and nothing is popping out, place under the foot a shoulder support table. Then press firmly, and leave it for three days, then release it;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And make him rest, until he becomes well.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with a dislocation and one seeks to restore it, many times death of the patient occurs:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not presumptuous in the treatment, if you are not wise in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and patient, do not be hasty;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and begin with soothing things like removing pus, and leave the patient in God's hands, if you do not see hope for their recovery;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, immediately reset the limb in its place, so that the pus and its discharge can occur.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is in its place, administer soothing things for pus removal, and treat the wound as it should be, using dried ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is a break during dislocation, and small bones are fractured, you should manage them as we have instructed in simple illnesses;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard against entering the path of fear, as I have said, for this befits you to act according to your Creator, and through knowledge arm yourself and protect your body.
